學習目標 / Learning Objectives

  • EN: Define a Controlled Temperature Chamber (CTC) and explain why temperature mapping is critical for GMP compliance.
  • 中文：能定義「受控溫度腔體」(CTC)，並說明溫度繪圖對 GMP 合規的重要性。
  • EN: Identify the key regulatory frameworks governing CTCs — EU GDP, WHO TRS 961, USP <659>, PIC/S PE 011.
  • 中文：識別管制 CTC 的主要法規框架，包括 EU GDP、WHO TRS 961、USP <659> 及 PIC/S PE 011。
  • EN: List the minimum elements required in a User Requirements Specification (URS) for a CTC and explain the URS-to-qualification traceability chain.
  • 中文：列出 CTC 用戶需求規格 (URS) 的最低必要內容，並說明 URS 至確效的可追溯鏈。
  • EN: Distinguish between the six main CTC types and match each type to its temperature range, typical products, and qualification strategy.
  • 中文：區別六種主要 CTC 類型，並能將各類型與其溫度範圍、典型產品及確效策略對應。
  • EN: Apply a CDMO perspective: multi-client storage segregation, incoming inspection staging areas, and stability program design across CTC types.
  • 中文：應用 CDMO 視角：多客戶儲存隔離、進廠檢驗暫存區管理，及跨腔體類型的安定性計畫設計。
1

Chapter 1 — Introduction | 導論

What is a CTC? Why does this guide exist? | 什麼是受控溫度腔體？本指南的存在意義

Original Text (ISPE 2016)

A Controlled Temperature Chamber is defined as a system, unit, equipment, or room in which the environmental conditions (usually temperature) of a chamber are controlled/maintained/regulated to meet specific user requirements.

The ISPE Good Practice Guide: Controlled Temperature Chamber Mapping and Monitoring expands on the ISPE Concept Paper on Controlled Temperature Chamber Mapping to include topics such as:

  • Commissioning
  • Testing strategies
  • Acceptance criteria
  • Qualification approaches
  • System monitoring
  • Operational issues
  • Periodic review
"Types of Controlled Temperature Chambers considered by this guide range from purchased Commercial Off the Shelf items, such as freezers and incubators, walk-in cold rooms and walk-in freezers, to custom built units, such as warehouses."

This Guide provides industry good practice for the temperature mapping of controlled temperature chambers, development of test acceptance criteria and a risk based approach to practices for periodic review of system performance.

CDMO Commentary | 製藥 CDMO 解析

核心定義：受控溫度腔體 (CTC)

簡單說，CTC 就是「任何你刻意把溫度鎖在某個範圍內的空間或設備」。從一台桌上型冷藏庫到一整棟冷凍倉庫，只要有溫度控制就算。關鍵詞：controlled / maintained / regulated。

在 CDMO 環境裡，CTC 的種類特別多元——你可能同時管理：原料冷凍庫 (-20°C)、成品冷藏區 (2–8°C)、安定性腔體 (25°C/60%RH)，以及室溫倉庫 (15–25°C)。每種都是 CTC，每種都需要映射。

比喻：CTC 就像恆溫保險箱

想像你把昂貴的藥品放進一個保險箱——這個保險箱不只要鎖住，還要確保裡面的溫度永遠在規定範圍。「溫度映射」就是在整個箱子的每個角落放溫度計，確認沒有任何角落偷偷超溫或過冷。

重點提示：這本指南的地位

ISPE GPG 不是法規，它是產業良好實踐。監管機關（EMA、FDA、WHO）不強制你跟它走，但當你在稽核中說「我們依照 ISPE GPG」，這是強有力的防禦性聲明——代表你與業界最佳實踐對齊。

思考問題 1

你的廠房裡有哪些設備或空間符合「CTC」定義？列出至少三種，並說明它們各自的溫度控制目的。

Which equipment or rooms in your facility qualify as CTCs? List at least three and describe their temperature control purpose.

1.1

1.1 Purpose and Objectives | 目的與目標

Why was this guide developed? | 本指南的開發動機

Original Text (ISPE 2016)

With the increasing complexity of global distribution for medicines requiring controlled temperatures and the recently introduced regulations, the ISPE Good Practice Guide was developed by an industry team in order to provide guidance on good practices for:

  • Definition of requirements (producing a user requirements document)
  • Design
  • Purchasing
  • Commissioning (including temperature mapping)
  • Qualification
  • Maintenance of controlled temperature chambers, warehouses, and refrigerated storage areas

These systems are used to store raw material, work in progress, or finished product, and operate under current Good Manufacturing Practice.

The approach described is consistent with that described in the ISPE Good Practice Guide: Cold Chain Management.

CDMO Commentary | CDMO 解析

生命週期視角：從 URS 到維護

這個清單就是 CTC 的完整生命週期。注意順序：先定義需求 (URS)，再設計，再購買——不是買了設備再去想規格。這在 CDMO 環境中尤其重要，因為很多公司是「先買設備，後補文件」，這會造成確效困難。

CDMO 情境應用

在合約製藥廠，你可能同時為 5 個以上的客戶儲存不同溫度條件的原料與成品。每批原料都有其溫度儲存要求（客戶 SOP 或 CoA 規定），而你的 CTC 必須能夠証明它在整個儲存期間維持了正確的條件。

這就是為什麼溫度映射記錄是 CDMO 客戶稽核中最常被要求的文件之一。

冷鏈管理的連結

本指南與 ISPE Cold Chain Management GPG 配套使用。CTC 是冷鏈的靜態節點——產品在倉庫和工廠內的存儲環節。運輸屬於另一份指南的範疇，但原則相通。

1.2

1.2 Scope | 適用範圍

What is IN and OUT of scope | 範圍界定

Original Text (ISPE 2016)

This Guide provides guidance on Controlled Temperature Chambers operating under Current Good Manufacturing Practices (CGMPs). Types of Controlled Temperature Chambers considered by this guide include:

  • Purchased "commercial off the shelf" items (such as freezers, refrigerators, and incubators)
  • Warm rooms designed to maintain consistent temperatures
  • Ovens
  • Custom built units, such as controlled room temperature environments (e.g., warehouses, walk-in cold rooms and freezers)

This Guide does not include systems designed for heating/cooling of material such as blast freezers, although some of the concepts described may be useful when commissioning/qualifying these systems.

CDMO Commentary | CDMO 解析

範圍劃分的重要性

指南明確把「儲存用 CTC」和「加熱/冷卻製程設備」分開。這個分界很實用：

  • In Scope（在範圍內）：冰箱、冷凍庫、安定性腔體、冷藏室、室溫倉庫
  • Out of Scope（範圍外）：速凍機 (blast freezer)、滅菌烘箱（用於製程）

但注意：「some concepts may be useful」——也就是說，你可以把映射原則應用到製程設備，只是不在本指南的主要討論範圍。

cGMP vs GDP 的界線

本指南聚焦在 cGMP 環境（製造廠的儲存）。GDP（Good Distribution Practice）管的是從工廠出門後的運輸與配送。兩者有重疊，但 CDMO 首要關注的是廠內 GMP 合規。

比喻：儲存 vs 製程

把食材放在冰箱保鮮 = CTC（本指南範圍）。把食材放進炒鍋加熱 = 製程設備（不在範圍）。本指南只管「保鮮冰箱」，不管「炒菜的鍋」。

1.3

1.3 Benefits | 使用本指南的效益

Why follow this guide? | 為什麼要遵循本指南？

Original Text (ISPE 2016)

There is an increased regulatory interest in cold chain driven by the growing number of products requiring controlled temperature shipping and storage, the complexity of the distribution network for the products and governmental requirements for distribution of vaccines.

This is reflected in the recent revisions to the related regulatory guidance. Utilizing this Guide provides a number of benefits in an area where there is little authoritative guidance, including:

  • Provision of industry good practice for the temperature mapping of controlled temperature chambers, considering the impact of load, and the use of the data to determine the location and number of monitoring sensors
  • Development of test acceptance criteria
  • A risk based approach to practices for periodic review of system performance

CDMO Commentary | CDMO 解析

監管趨勢：冷鏈的全球化壓力

生物製劑（mAb、疫苗、基因治療）在全球藥品市場的比例快速增長，這類產品幾乎都需要嚴格的溫度控制。監管機關（EMA、WHO、TFDA）對冷鏈的稽核強度也隨之提升。

對 CDMO 來說，這代表：你的客戶（BigPharma）在稽核你的設施時，CTC 映射記錄是必查項目。

三大具體效益

  • 效益 1：有標準化的映射方法論，知道要放幾個感測器、放哪裡
  • 效益 2：有明確的接受標準 (acceptance criteria) 框架，讓你知道「通過」的定義
  • 效益 3：有風險導向的定期複審頻率，不用每年都全面重做映射

思考問題 2

你的廠目前如何決定冷藏庫溫度監測感測器的位置？這個決策是基於映射數據，還是基於習慣？

How does your site currently decide where to place temperature monitoring sensors in cold storage? Is this based on mapping data or convention?

1.4

1.4 Regulatory Guidance | 法規指引

Key regulations and standards governing CTCs | 管制 CTC 的主要法規與標準

Original Text (ISPE 2016)

Regulatory guidance covering Controlled Temperature Chambers issued or updated at time of publication includes:

  1. HPRA: Guide to Good Distribution Practice of Medicinal Products for Human Use
  2. HPRA: Guide to Control and Monitoring of Storage and Transportation Temperature Conditions for Medicinal Products and Active Substances
  3. EMA Guidelines (7 March 2013) on Good Distribution Practice of Medicinal Products for Human Use
  4. PIC/S Guide PE 011-1 to Good Distribution Practice for Medicinal Products

Also see:

  1. European Commission Guidelines (5 November 2013) on Good Distribution Practice
  2. Health Canada GUI-0069: Guidelines for Temperature Control of Drug Products during Storage and Transportation
  3. WHO Technical Report Series No. 961, Annex 9: Model Guidance for the Storage and Transport of Time- and Temperature-Sensitive Pharmaceutical Products
  4. MCA Part II, Chapter 6: Control and Monitoring of Storage and Transit Temperatures

In the United States Pharmacopeia (USP):

  1. USP <659> Packaging and Storage Requirements

法規解析與 CDMO 應用

法規層次架構

這些法規可以分為三個層次：

  • 強制性法規：EU GDP Guidelines（EMA/歐盟委員會）— 在歐盟市場銷售產品必須合規
  • 準強制性指引：WHO TRS 961 — WHO 會員國的監管基礎，TFDA 多以此為參考
  • 產品規格性標準：USP <659> — 定義了「冷藏」「冷凍」「室溫」等術語的官方溫度範圍

WHO TRS 961 Annex 9 的關鍵要求

WHO TRS 961 Annex 9 對「時間和溫度敏感產品」（TTSP）的儲存和運輸提供了最完整的指引，包括：

  • 溫度映射的最低要求（感測器數量、持續時間）
  • 溫度偏差的處理程序
  • 風險評估的應用
  • 再驗證的觸發條件

對於出口到新興市場（非洲、東南亞）的 CDMO，WHO 指引往往是當地 NRA 的稽核基礎。

USP <659> 溫度定義

USP <659> 是客戶 CoA 中「儲存條件」欄位的法律依據：

  • Freezer（冷凍）: -25°C to -10°C
  • Refrigerator（冷藏）: 2°C to 8°C
  • Cool（涼爽）: 8°C to 15°C
  • Controlled Room Temperature（受控室溫）: 20°C to 25°C

當客戶說「Store at 2–8°C」，這就是 USP 標準，你的 CTC 必須証明能維持在這個範圍內。

思考問題 3

你的廠目前在 CTC 確效文件中引用了哪些法規？這些法規是否涵蓋了你出口市場的要求？

Which regulations does your site currently cite in CTC qualification documents? Do they cover the requirements of your export markets?

1.5

1.5 Key Concepts / Key Terms | 關鍵概念與術語

Commissioning, Qualification, and Rounding Rules | 試運轉、確效與數值捨入規則

Original Text (ISPE 2016)

Commissioning

A well planned, documented, and managed engineering approach to the start-up and turnover of facilities, systems, and equipment to the End-User, that results in a safe and functional environment that meets established design requirements and stakeholder expectations.

Qualification

Activities undertaken to demonstrate that utilities and equipment are suitable for their intended use and perform properly. (FDA)

Rounding of Temperature Values

This Guide follows USP <32> Section 7.20 Rounding Rules:

"When rounding is required, consider only one digit in the decimal place to the right of the last place in the limit expression. If this digit is smaller than 5, it is eliminated and the preceding digit is unchanged. If this digit is equal to or greater than 5, it is eliminated and the preceding digit is increased by 1."

術語深度解析

試運轉 vs 確效：傻傻分不清？

這兩個詞在廠內常被混用，但 ISPE 的定義非常清楚：

  • Commissioning（試運轉）：工程導向，確保設備「能動」且符合設計規格。重點：Does it work as designed?
  • Qualification（確效）：法規導向，証明設備「適合其預定用途」。重點：Is it fit for GMP use?

試運轉先做，確效後做。試運轉的文件可以支撐確效，但不能取代確效。

比喻：試運轉 vs 確效

新車交車前的出廠測試 = Commissioning（確認引擎能動、煞車有效）。

駕訓班的路考 = Qualification（在特定條件下証明你能安全駕駛）。

你可以通過出廠測試但路考失敗（設備能動但不符合 GMP 要求）；你也可以路考通過但不會修車（符合 GMP 但日常維護不佳）。

數值捨入規則的實際意義

這個看似微小的規則在實際操作中非常重要。舉例：

  • 上限 8°C，測量到 8.4°C → 捨入後 = 8°C → 通過
  • 上限 8°C，測量到 8.5°C → 捨入後 = 9°C → 失敗

在設定警報上限和確效接受標準時，這個規則決定了你在「邊界值」的判斷——不能隨意四捨五入。

2

Chapter 2 — Related Standards | 相關標準

International standards applicable to CTCs | 適用於受控溫度腔體的國際標準

Original Text (ISPE 2016) — Section 2 & 2.1

Regulatory guidance for Good Distribution Practice (GDP) is updated on a regular basis. There is normally a requirement to demonstrate that product is being stored in the appropriate conditions. This can be accomplished through the mapping that all storage locations used in the Controlled Temperature Chamber remain within the defined conditions.

2.1 Standards

There are no Standards written specifically for Controlled Temperature Chambers as used in the Pharmaceutical and Biotechnology industry. Available Standards are written for Environmental Test Chambers and Stability Chambers. Although the same principles may be applied, the details of how the systems are to be used in an operational environment should also be considered.

A list of applicable Standards known at time of publication:

Japan:

  • JTM K 01 — Temperature and Humidity Chambers – Test and Indication Method for Performance
  • JTM K 03 — Environmental Temperature and Humidity Rooms – Test and Indication Method for Performance
  • JTM K 05 — High Temperature Chambers – Test and Indication Method for Performance

France:

  • FD X15-140 — Measurement of Air Moisture – Climatic and Thermostatic Chambers – Characterization and Verification

Germany:

  • DIN 12880 — Electrical Laboratory Devices – Heating Ovens and Incubators

Australia:

  • AS 2853 — Enclosures – Temperature Controlled Performance Testing and Grading

IEC:

  • IEC 60068 — Environmental Testing Series

Controlled Temperature Chambers used in the Pharmaceutical and Biotechnology industry are usually used for either long term storage (stability) or for short term storage Work in Progress (WIP)/distribution warehousing storage.

Note: China (PRC) and South Korea use Good Supply Practice (GSP) rather than GDP.

標準解析與應用

關鍵認知：沒有專屬藥廠的 CTC 標準

ISPE 在此坦白承認了一個重要事實：目前沒有任何國際標準是專門為製藥 CTC 寫的。現有標準都是為「環境測試腔體」或「安定性腔體」所寫，製藥業只是「借用」這些標準的原則。

這正是 ISPE GPG 存在的理由——填補了法規要求和工業標準之間的空白。

比喻：借用標準就像穿別人的制服

IEC 60068 是為電子工廠設計的，製藥廠「借穿」它就像穿了稍微不合身的制服。原則可以用，但細節（如感測器位置、典型負荷條件）需要結合藥廠的實際使用場景調整。

這就是為什麼 ISPE GPG 強調：「although the same principles may be applied, the details of how the systems are to be used in an operational environment should also be considered.」

兩種主要使用模式

ISPE 在章節末尾點出了 CTC 的兩種核心使用場景：

  • 長期儲存（安定性）：需要高穩定性、嚴格的溫濕度控制，映射要求最嚴格（ICH Q1A 條件：25°C/60%RH、40°C/75%RH 等）
  • 短期儲存（WIP / 倉儲）：通量大、開門頻繁、負荷變化大，映射需要考慮最壞情況（worst case loading）

不同使用模式，映射策略不同——這是後續章節的核心主題。

GSP vs GDP：亞太市場的差異

指南腳注提醒：中國和韓國使用 GSP（Good Supply Practice）而非 GDP。對於台灣 CDMO 出口到中國或韓國的產品，需確認客戶要求是否有 GSP 特定要求。台灣 TFDA 本身以 PIC/S 為基準，與 EU GDP 高度對齊。

思考問題 4

你的廠的安定性腔體確效文件中，引用了哪些標準？這些標準是否足以支撐歐盟客戶的稽核？

Which standards does your site reference in stability chamber qualification documents? Are they sufficient to support EU customer audits?

3

Chapter 3 — User Requirements Specification | 用戶需求規格書

Write the URS before you buy — not after | 先寫 URS，再採購設備

The URS is the contract between what the business needs and what the equipment must deliver — write it before you buy, not after.

URS 是業務需求與設備交付之間的合約——在採購之前寫，而不是之後補。

Original Text (ISPE 2016) — Chapter 3

A User Requirements Specification (URS) is a document that defines the user's functional requirements for equipment or systems. By defining specific requirements in the URS, and not how those requirements are met, the designer is given freedom to provide the optimum design solution to meet the requirements.

Aspects to be considered in relation to stored material include:

  • Unit capacity (i.e., quantity and nature of the material to be stored)
  • Whether the unit is providing cooling or heating (i.e., preconditioning) of the stored material, and if so:
    • What criteria have to be met, e.g., maximum load size, specific heat capacity supply, temperature, heating/cooling time?
    • How long and how frequently is the door to load/unload the unit open?
    • Which environmental conditions are critical, e.g., light/temperature/humidity?

Qualification is intended to demonstrate through testing (verification) that the requirements specified in the URS have been met. Confirmation that the user requirements have been met should be traceable in the qualification documentation.

Appendix 1 provides discussion of typical content and an example of a URS for a cold room.

"Note: information included in specifications or the purchase order general requirements (such as manuals, training, spare parts) are not included in the URS to avoid duplication; the URS should be a simple concise definition of the user requirements."

For a standard "catalogue" item, the URS may be developed in the form of the purchase order.

URS 深度解析 | CDMO 應用

什麼是 URS？為什麼它如此重要？

URS 是整個設備生命週期的起點文件。它回答一個核心問題：「這台設備需要做到什麼？」

注意 ISPE 的細微但重要的說法：URS 定義什麼(what)，不定義如何(how)。這給供應商設計自由度，同時確保最終交付符合使用者真實需求。

比喻：URS 就像建築設計委託書

你委託建築師蓋房子，你說「我需要一個能住4人、有兩個浴室、夏天室內不超過26°C的房子，預算500萬」——這是 URS 的精神。

你不說「用什麼牌子的磚頭」或「空調要裝在哪個位置」——那是設計規格 (Design Specification, DS) 和安裝規格 (Installation Specification, IS) 的工作。

CDMO 冷藏庫 URS 必要元素

以下是一個 CDMO 2–8°C 冷藏庫 URS 的典型必要元素：

URS → 確效的可追溯鏈

ISPE 強調：確效文件必須能可追溯地証明每一條 URS 要求都已被滿足。這代表你的 OQ/PQ 協議中，每個測試項目都應該有一個對應的 URS 編號。

如果你的確效報告找不到某條 URS 要求的対应測試，這就是稽核發現 (observation) 的來源。

小型設備的特殊處理

對於標準目錄品（如小型實驗室冰箱），ISPE 允許 URS 以採購單的形式呈現——也就是採購單上的技術規格就是 URS。但對於走入式冷凍庫、大型倉庫等客製化設備，仍需要獨立的正式 URS 文件。

思考問題 5

你的廠上次購買冷藏設備時，是先寫 URS 還是先選設備？如果是後者，你如何補救確效文件中的可追溯性？

When your site last purchased refrigeration equipment, was the URS written first or the equipment selected first? If the latter, how did you address traceability gaps in the qualification documentation?

URS Element Checklist | URS 要素核查清單

Performance Requirements | 性能要求

  • Temperature range defined (min/max) | 溫度範圍已定義（最低/最高）
  • Temperature uniformity requirement | 溫度均勻性要求
  • Temperature recovery time after door opening | 開門後溫度回復時間
  • Humidity control (if applicable) | 濕度控制（如適用）
  • Light protection requirements | 避光要求（如適用）
  • Vibration/noise limits (for sensitive products) | 振動/噪音限制

Capacity & Loading | 容量與負荷

  • Maximum storage volume/weight | 最大儲存體積/重量
  • Typical load configuration | 典型負荷配置
  • Door opening frequency and duration | 開門頻率與時間
  • Number of access points/doors | 進出口/門數量
  • Shelving or pallet racking requirements | 貨架或棧板架要求

Monitoring & Alarms | 監測與警報

  • Continuous temperature monitoring requirement | 持續溫度監測要求
  • Alarm setpoints (high/low/rate of change) | 警報設定點（高/低/變化速率）
  • Alarm notification method (visual/audible/remote) | 警報通知方式
  • Data recording interval and retention period | 數據記錄間隔與保存期
  • Data integrity requirements (21 CFR Part 11 / EU Annex 11) | 數據完整性要求

Access & Safety | 進入管制與安全

  • Access control requirement (key/card/biometric) | 進入管制要求
  • Segregation requirements (multi-client) | 隔離要求（多客戶環境）
  • Emergency power backup | 緊急電力備援
  • Safety interlocks (anti-entrapment for walk-ins) | 安全連鎖（走入式防困人）
  • Utility connections (power, drain) | 公用設施連接（電力、排水）

Environmental Conditions | 環境條件

  • Ambient temperature range at installation site | 安裝地點環境溫度範圍
  • Ambient humidity at installation site | 安裝地點環境濕度
  • Clean room classification (if applicable) | 潔淨室分級（如適用）
  • Seismic/structural requirements | 抗震/結構要求

Maintenance & Qualification | 維護與確效

  • Maintenance access requirements | 維護可及性要求
  • Defrost cycle requirements (no product exposure) | 除霜循環要求（不影響產品）
  • Calibration access for sensors | 感測器校準可及性
  • Qualification (IQ/OQ/PQ) expected | 預期的確效活動（IQ/OQ/PQ）
  • Documentation package requirements | 文件包要求
4

Chapter 4 — Types of Controlled Temperature Chamber | 受控溫度腔體類型

Overview: how CTC type drives qualification strategy | 腔體類型如何決定確效策略

Original Text (ISPE 2016) — Chapter 4 Overview

The ISPE Good Practice Guide recognizes the following main types of Controlled Temperature Chambers used in pharmaceutical and biotechnology manufacturing and storage:

  • 4.1 Freezers — Ultra-low (-80°C), standard (-20°C), and other sub-zero temperature units. Used for long-term storage of biological materials, vaccines, and temperature-sensitive APIs.
  • 4.2 Refrigerators — Units maintaining 2–8°C. The most common CTC for finished pharmaceutical products, including biologics, vaccines, and drug substances.
  • 4.3 Cold Rooms (Walk-in) — Large-scale refrigerated spaces, typically 2–8°C, designed for bulk storage of materials with high throughput and frequent access.
  • 4.4 Stability Chambers — Chambers designed to maintain precise temperature and humidity conditions for ICH Q1A stability testing. Typical conditions: 25°C/60%RH (long-term), 40°C/75%RH (accelerated), 30°C/65%RH (intermediate).
  • Incubators / Incubator Shakers — Units for microbiological and cell culture applications, typically 30–37°C.
  • Controlled Temperature Rooms — Large spaces maintained at controlled room temperature (typically 15–25°C per USP) for ambient storage of products not requiring refrigeration.

The type of CTC determines the applicable testing strategy, the number and location of mapping sensors, the qualification approach, and the frequency of periodic re-qualification.

CDMO 視角：腔體類型的戰略意義

為什麼腔體類型決定確效策略？

不同類型的 CTC 有根本性的差異：

  • 體積差異：從桌上型實驗室冰箱到千坪倉庫，感測器需求完全不同
  • 使用模式：安定性腔體幾乎不開門；走入式冷藏室每天進出數十次
  • 溫度範圍：-80°C 超低溫凍庫和 25°C 室溫倉庫的映射挑戰截然不同
  • 法規要求：安定性腔體需符合 ICH Q1A；倉庫要符合 GDP

CDMO 特殊場景：多客戶儲存的複雜性

在合約製藥廠，一個冷藏區域可能同時儲存：

  • 客戶 A 的原料藥（需要 2–8°C，進口檢驗後暫存）
  • 客戶 B 的半成品（需要 2–8°C，等待 QC 放行）
  • 客戶 C 的成品（需要 2–8°C，等待出貨）

這三種物料可能在同一個冷藏室，但必須有明確的物理或視覺隔離。映射時必須証明整個空間——包括每個客戶的存放區——都在 2–8°C 之間。

CDMO 進廠檢驗暫存區

一個常被忽略的 CTC 是進廠檢驗暫存區（Incoming Inspection Staging Area）。當需要冷藏的原料到廠後，等待 QC 抽樣和放行期間，它必須存放在符合儲存條件的區域。

這個暫存區往往是一個獨立的小型冷藏庫或冷藏室的隔離區域，它同樣是 CTC，同樣需要映射和確效。

思考問題 6

你的廠的進廠冷藏原料，從卸貨到通過 QC 放行進入正式冷藏庫這段期間，存放在哪裡？這個區域有映射記錄嗎？

In your facility, where do incoming cold-chain materials sit between receiving dock and QC release into the main cold storage? Does that staging area have mapping records?

CTC Type Comparison Table | 受控溫度腔體類型比較表

CDMO-Specific Scenarios | CDMO 特定應用場景

場景 1：多客戶安定性計畫

你同時為 8 個客戶管理安定性樣品，使用同一台 40°C/75%RH 腔體。映射文件必須証明腔體在滿載（所有客戶樣品）條件下仍符合 ICH 條件。

關鍵要求：映射時使用最大預期負荷；每個客戶的安定性協議中引用同一份確效報告是否合適？需要個別客戶確認嗎？

場景 2：進廠原料暫存

供應商運來需要冷藏的原料，但 QC 採樣完成需要 48–72 小時。這段期間原料必須存放在符合條件的 CTC 中。

常見問題：進廠暫存區往往沒有獨立的確效記錄，或與正式冷藏庫混用。這是稽核中的高風險發現點。

場景 3：無菌填充前的原料暫存

蛋白質藥液在灌裝前需要在 2–8°C 下短暫儲存（通常不超過 24–48 小時）。這個存儲容器（不鏽鋼桶或生物反應袋）的存放環境是 CTC。

特殊考量：這是製造環境（不只是倉儲），需同時符合 GMP 潔淨室要求和 CTC 溫度要求。

CTC Type to Qualification Approach | 腔體類型對應確效方法

Practice Questions | 綜合練習問題

Test your understanding of Chapters 1–4 | 測試你對第 1–4 章的理解

Conceptual Questions | 概念問題

Q1 — CTC Definition

A company uses a standard household refrigerator to store reagents used in QC testing. Is this a CTC? Does it require temperature mapping? What factors would determine the extent of qualification required?

一間公司使用家用冰箱儲存 QC 測試用試劑。這算是 CTC 嗎？需要溫度映射嗎？哪些因素決定確效程度？

Q2 — Commissioning vs Qualification

Your new walk-in cold room vendor has completed commissioning and provided a commissioning report showing all temperatures within 2–8°C. Can you use this report as your OQ? Why or why not?

供應商完成走入式冷藏室的試運轉，報告顯示溫度符合 2–8°C。這份報告可以作為你的 OQ 嗎？為什麼？

Q3 — URS Timing

Your site purchased a -20°C freezer urgently to support a new client project, and the URS was written after installation. What are the qualification risks? How would you remediate this situation?

你的廠緊急採購了一台 -20°C 冷凍庫，URS 在安裝後才寫。有哪些確效風險？如何補救？

Q4 — Temperature Rounding

Your 2–8°C refrigerator shows a maximum reading of 8.45°C. Applying the USP rounding rule, does this represent a temperature excursion? What about 8.50°C?

你的 2–8°C 冰箱顯示最高讀數 8.45°C。依 USP 捨入規則，這是溫度偏差嗎？8.50°C 呢？

Application Questions | 應用問題

Q5 — CTC Type Selection

A new biologic drug substance arrives at your CDMO requiring storage at -80°C. You currently only have -20°C freezers. List five items you would include in the URS for a new ultra-low freezer, and explain why each is important.

新的生物製劑原料藥需要 -80°C 儲存，你目前只有 -20°C 冷凍庫。列出新超低溫冷凍庫 URS 中的五項要求，並說明每項的重要性。

Q6 — Regulatory Alignment

A European client is auditing your CDMO and asks: "Which GDP guideline do you follow for your cold storage areas?" Your site currently cites only ICH Q1A in CTC documents. Is this sufficient? What would be the correct answer?

歐洲客戶稽核你的 CDMO，問：「你們冷儲區域依循哪個 GDP 指引？」你的廠目前只引用 ICH Q1A。這樣足夠嗎？正確答案是什麼？

Q7 — Multi-Client Scenarios

You have one stability chamber running at 25°C/60%RH for five different clients' stability programs. Client F wants to add 200 additional samples that would fill the chamber to 95% capacity. What questions would you ask before agreeing, and what re-mapping may be required?

你有一台安定性腔體同時為五個客戶運行安定性計畫。客戶F想新增200份樣品，將腔體填充至95%。你會問哪些問題？需要重新映射嗎？

Q8 — Standards Gap Analysis

ISPE states there are no standards written specifically for pharmaceutical CTCs. Given this gap, how should your site justify the qualification approach for a new walk-in cold room to a regulatory inspector?

ISPE 指出沒有專為製藥 CTC 制定的標準。面對這個空白，你如何向法規稽查員論證新走入式冷藏室的確效方法？

Scenario Question | 情境題 Q9 — CDMO Cold Storage Review

You are the QA Director at a CDMO. During an internal audit, you find the following issues. For each, identify (a) which chapter of the ISPE CTC GPG is most relevant, (b) the regulatory risk, and (c) your recommended corrective action:

  1. The -20°C freezer URS was never created — only a purchase order exists.
  2. The stability chamber qualification references only AS 2853, with no mention of ICH Q1A or EU GDP.
  3. The walk-in cold room temperature monitoring sensors are placed "where they fit" with no mapping data to justify the locations.
  4. The incoming inspection staging refrigerator has never been qualified — the team says "it's only temporary storage."

你是一家 CDMO 的 QA 總監。內部稽核中發現以下問題。針對每個問題，識別：(a) ISPE CTC GPG 最相關的章節，(b) 法規風險，(c) 你建議的改善措施。

Regulatory Reference Summary | 法規引用快速參考

Key citations for CTC qualification and storage compliance

SUM

Chapter Summary | 章節重點摘要

Key takeaways from Chapters 1–4 | 第 1–4 章核心要點

Chapter 1 — Introduction 導論

  • CTC = 任何溫度受控的設備或空間，從小冰箱到大倉庫都算
  • 本指南的定位：產業良好實踐（非法規），但具強力防禦效力
  • Commissioning（試運轉）≠ Qualification（確效）：前者工程導向，後者法規導向
  • 溫度數值捨入遵循 USP <32> 規則，邊界值判斷不能隨意

Chapter 2 — Related Standards 相關標準

  • 沒有專為製藥 CTC 制定的國際標準——空白由 ISPE GPG 填補
  • 現有標準（IEC 60068、AS 2853、DIN 12880）是借用，原則適用但細節需調整
  • GDP（Good Distribution Practice）是主要監管框架；中國/韓國使用 GSP
  • CTC 用途分兩類：長期儲存（安定性）vs 短期 WIP/倉儲，映射策略不同

Chapter 3 — URS 用戶需求規格

  • URS 定義「需要什麼」(WHAT)，不定義「如何做到」(HOW)
  • 先寫 URS，再採購設備——這是生命週期管理的正確順序
  • 確效文件必須可追溯地対应每一條 URS 要求
  • 標準目錄品可用採購單形式作為 URS；客製化設備需獨立 URS 文件

Chapter 4 — CTC Types 腔體類型

  • 六種主要類型：超低溫凍庫、標準冷凍庫、冷藏庫、走入式冷藏室、安定性腔體、受控溫度室
  • 腔體類型決定映射策略、感測器數量/位置、確效方法和再確效頻率
  • CDMO 特殊挑戰：多客戶隔離、進廠暫存、無菌製程前暫存
  • 每種腔體類型對應不同的主要法規框架

The URS is the contract between what the business needs and what the equipment must deliver.

Write it before you buy. Map it before you use it. Review it before it fails you.

在採購前寫好 URS。在使用前完成映射。在問題發生前定期複審。

  • 列出安裝階段四大類試運行活動

4.1

Freezers / 冷凍庫

-20°C to -196°C storage — design, defrost cycles, and GMP monitoring requirements

Original Text (ISPE 2016, pp.16–18)

4.1 Freezers

Freezers are used for short to long term preservation of pharmaceutical and biopharmaceutical materials, including: Active Pharmaceutical Ingredients (APIs), process intermediates, stability samples, laboratory materials, and cell banks. Temperature uniformity is maintained within a qualified range to ensure product quality is preserved. Freezers with set points ranging from -20°C to -80°C (-4°F to -112°F) are frequently used.

Operation can be controlled via a temperature controller that maintains the locally configured temperature set point and also provides a local alarm. Manual defrost chambers are usually equipped with the general freezer refrigeration components of: compressor, receiver, condenser, evaporator, tubing, insulation, and structural support.

The refrigerant compressors are usually hermetically sealed for integrity. The evaporator is typically a tube and fin design. The chamber control monitors interior temperature using a permanently installed thermocouple or Resistance Temperature Detector (RTD) — referred to as the control probe. Typically, the control probe is calibrated at the factory based on the temperature at the geometric center of the chamber. The evaporator is usually located within the upper portion of the chamber interior and chamber temperature uniformity is obtained through natural air circulation.

For units with automatic defrost, the control actuates an automatic defrost cycle at a predetermined frequency (typically 6 to 24 hours) to minimize ice accumulation. The defrost cycle is terminated by: elapsed time, evaporator coil temperature set point, or a combination of time and temperature. The frequency of defrost is adjustable to allow for conditions of use (frequency of door openings, length of time for door openings, and exterior air humidity level).

For GMP applications these systems should be monitored by an independent system. It can be difficult to calibrate the system control sensor, and the use of an independent system allows routine calibration, and the flexibility to place the sensor in a location that measures the "worst case" temperature. This system is used as the quality "system of record" to provide the data used to demonstrate that materials are being stored at the specified conditions.

4.1.1 Conditioning / Blast Freezers

Facilities may process large quantities of bulk product that needs to be frozen from ambient conditions to a specified temperature, e.g., -70°C, prior to transfer into -70°C storage locations. Dedicated conditioning freezers are needed to perform this function, as storage freezers are not capable of handling the large volume of product and significant temperature disparity without potentially compromising the temperature of stored material. This type of equipment is outside the scope of this guide.

4.1.2 Liquid Nitrogen Freezers

Used for storage of material below -120°C (-184°F), e.g., cell banks. If materials are immersed into liquid nitrogen, they eventually assume the temperature of the liquid (-196°C). Materials stored in the vapor above the liquid become warmer as they are moved away from the liquid (up to -120°C). The temperature of the vapor can be changed by varying the amount of liquid nitrogen in the chamber.

解析與 CDMO 情境應用

比喻：控制探針 vs. 獨立監控系統

冷凍庫原廠內建的控制探針就像汽車儀表板的油溫表 — 它讓引擎運作，但不能用來做法規報告。獨立監控系統才是你的品質記錄系統，相當於行車記錄器，提供可稽核的連續數據。

ISPE 明確要求：GMP 應用必須有獨立監控系統作為「品質記錄系統 (system of record)」。控制探針僅維持設定點，獨立系統才用於合規報告。

CDMO 多客戶情境：冷凍庫獨立監控的重要性

在多客戶 CDMO 環境中，同一台 -80°C 冷凍庫可能同時存放三個不同客戶的 API 樣品。獨立監控系統的數據需能：

  • 按時間戳追溯每次門開啟事件
  • 顯示除霜週期期間的溫度波動是否影響儲存物
  • 提供客戶專屬的偏差記錄（需按客戶區隔報告）
  • 支援批次放行決策的溫度合規佐證

獨立系統的感測器位置應設在「最差案例」位置（最可能超出限度的角落），而非幾何中心。

除霜週期對 GMP 的影響

除霜週期（每 6-24 小時）期間，蒸發器溫度短暫升高以融化積霜。監控系統必須：

  • 能區分除霜引起的短暫溫升與真實的設備異常
  • 確認除霜期間產品溫度仍在可接受範圍內
  • 在確認中記錄除霜週期對腔體溫度的實際影響

確認時需在除霜週期期間進行溫度 mapping，記錄其影響。

練習思考

  1. 您的廠房有一台 -80°C 冷凍庫，客戶要求提供過去 30 天的連續溫度記錄。如果只有原廠控制探針的日誌，為何這份記錄可能不被接受？
  2. 除霜頻率設定過低可能導致哪些 GMP 風險？設定過高又會有什麼問題？
  3. Blast Freezer（急凍庫）為何不在本指南範疇內？這對設備採購時的分類有何影響？
4.2

Refrigerators / 冷藏庫

2–8°C storage — forced air vs. convection, wire shelving, auto-defrost

Original Text (ISPE 2016, p.17)

4.2 Refrigerators

Refrigerators are typically used to store material and vaccines within a qualified range of 2°C to 8°C (36°F to 46°F). The capability of the equipment to achieve temperature uniformity should be considered when assigning the chamber set point.

Operation is typically controlled via a temperature controller that is used to maintain the locally configured temperature set point, and may also provide a local alarm. Refrigerators may be equipped with fans which cool via forced air circulation and utilize a hermetically sealed compressor and refrigeration system. Alternatively, refrigerators may use a heat exchanger located in the storage space, relying on convection to maintain an even temperature.

Refrigerators should have wire shelving to improve air circulation.

Refrigerators will usually automatically defrost the evaporator to maintain system performance. Evaporator defrost occurs by re-directing the hot refrigerant gas into the evaporator coil for a short time to melt any ice/frost accumulation.

解析與 CDMO 情境應用

冷藏庫核心設計要點

設定點 vs. 確認範圍：ISPE 提醒，設定點的選擇必須考量設備達到溫度均一性的能力。若設備在 4°C 設定下邊角溫度達到 8.5°C，則確認範圍可能無法涵蓋 2-8°C 規格，需調整設定點。

強制氣流 vs. 對流：有風扇的強制氣流型溫度均一性通常較佳，但門開啟時冷空氣流失更快。對流型較溫和，但對貨物擺放方式更敏感。

網架要求：ISPE 明確要求使用金屬網架而非實心板架，以確保空氣可在貨物之間流通，避免局部熱點。

比喻：設定點 ≠ 確認範圍

設定點是你告訴冷藏庫「維持在這個溫度」的指令，確認範圍是你用 mapping 資料證明腔體各處實際達到的溫度帶。兩者之間的差距，就是你在選設定點時必須預留的「緩衝帶」。若 mapping 顯示偏差 ±1.5°C，設定點應設在 4-5°C，而非緊貼 8°C 上限。

CDMO 多產品情境：冷藏庫分區管理

多客戶 CDMO 常見問題：不同客戶的疫苗、API 或中間體共用同一冷藏庫。建議：

  • 按客戶/產品劃定貨架區域，貼標識別
  • 確認時需模擬實際最大裝載量（worst case loading）
  • 實心板架違反 ISPE 建議，會在稽查中被提出
  • 每次新增客戶產品前確認擺放方式不會遮擋氣流

練習思考

  1. 一台 2-8°C 冷藏庫的溫度 mapping 顯示角落溫度為 8.3°C。這對設定點選擇有何影響？
  2. 客戶要求用實心金屬板架存放其產品（擔心落塵）。你如何回應這個要求，並找到符合雙方需求的解決方案？
  3. 強制氣流冷藏庫與對流冷藏庫在 mapping 策略上應有何不同考量？
4.3

Cold Rooms / 冷藏室（步入式）

Walk-in cold rooms — PLC control, redundant condensing, multi-sensor configurations

Original Text (ISPE 2016, pp.17–18)

4.3 Cold Rooms

Cold rooms are typically used for storage of material within a qualified range of 2°C to 8°C (36°F to 46°F). Cold rooms should be equipped with a refrigeration compressor/condensing unit. The air-cooled condensing unit is usually located outside, e.g., on the roof of the building. Cold rooms may be provided with redundant condensing systems, each capable of handling the total system load.

Walk-in cold rooms may be prefabricated, metal-clad structures, furnished and installed as self-contained units. These may include all essential refrigeration equipment, controls, air circulation, and other equipment necessary to reach the specified environmental conditions.

Cold room control systems usually consist of a local Programmable Logic Controller (PLC) to monitor and control the temperature within the cold room. Within the main chamber, the temperature may be measured by temperature sensors placed in different locations. One sensor should be routed to the main controller for controlling interior temperature. The second sensor should be connected to a monitoring system for temperature trending and alarm; for larger units there may be multiple monitoring sensors.

解析與 CDMO 情境應用

PLC 控制與 CSV 要求

冷藏室的 PLC 屬於電腦化系統，在 GMP 環境中可能觸發 21 CFR Part 11 或 Annex 11 的電腦化系統驗證 (CSV) 要求。關鍵考量：

  • PLC 軟體版本控制需納入變更管控
  • 存取權限管理（哪些人可修改設定點）
  • 審計追蹤（Audit trail）：記錄每次設定變更
  • 數據完整性：PLC 記錄的數據是否可被篡改？

若 PLC 涉及 GMP 關鍵數據，即使是冷藏室也需要進行 IQ/OQ 確認和 CSV 評估。

冗餘冷凝機組的 GMP 意義

冷藏室備有冗餘冷凝機組（各自能承擔完整負載）是高風險儲存物料的最佳實踐。試運行時必須測試：

  • 主機組切換至備援機組的時間
  • 切換過程中腔體溫度的波動範圍
  • 備援機組長期運作的穩定性（不能只是短暫啟動測試）

此數據在確認中同樣需要執行，以形成正式品質記錄。

練習思考

  1. 冷藏室的屋頂冷凝機組在夏天高溫環境下對冷藏室性能有何潛在影響？試運行時如何模擬最差案例？
  2. 如果冷藏室 PLC 的軟體升級了，這是否需要重新進行確認？依據什麼判斷？
  3. 一個 200 m³ 步入式冷藏室應配置多少個監控感測器？決定感測器數量的因素有哪些？
4.4

Stability Chambers & Incubators / 穩定性腔體與培養箱

ICH conditions 25/30/40°C — humidity, CO₂, multi-parameter control

Original Text (ISPE 2016, p.18)

4.4 Stability Chambers, Incubators / Incubator Shakers

Stability chambers are chambers that are designed to maintain a stable environment for incubating materials or holding samples. These may include cultures for microorganisms or cell culture and hybridization in production or Quality Control laboratories. The incubator may accommodate cell culture vessels from small tissue culture flasks to roller bottles and small spinner flasks.

A local controller should control system operation for process parameters such as temperature, humidity, and CO₂. Incubator shakers can also control shaker speed (Revolutions Per Minute (RPM) of the drive).

解析與 CDMO 情境應用

ICH 穩定性條件與對應腔體類型

穩定性腔體的 mapping 必須同時驗證溫度和濕度的均一性。

多參數控制的確認複雜度

與冷凍/冷藏庫相比，穩定性腔體和培養箱涉及多個受控參數：

  • 溫度：通常需要 ±2°C 以內的均一性
  • 濕度：需要 ±5% RH 以內的均一性（對機械也是挑戰）
  • CO₂ 濃度：培養箱特有，影響細胞培養 pH
  • 振盪速度 (RPM)：培養振盪箱的附加參數

每個參數都需要各自的感測器、校正記錄和確認測試。確認協議（IQ/OQ/PQ）的複雜度遠高於簡單儲存設備。

比喻：穩定性腔體是「人工氣候室」

穩定性腔體相當於一個精密人工氣候室，必須同時模擬全球不同地區的氣候條件。台灣的 CDMO 若要服務全球市場，通常需要配備能覆蓋所有 ICH 條件的穩定性腔體群。每個條件一旦偏離，整批穩定性數據可能需要被視為無效，對客戶申請影響巨大。

練習思考

  1. 穩定性腔體在溫度 mapping 時，是否需要同時進行濕度 mapping？這對感測器配置有何要求？
  2. 一台培養箱同時控制溫度、CO₂ 和轉速，當轉速感測器發生故障時，是否需要執行設備偏差報告？
  3. 台灣市場的新藥申請需要哪些 ICH 穩定性條件？這對穩定性腔體的採購規格有何影響？
"Commissioning is the engineering proof; qualification is the regulatory proof — both are necessary, they are not redundant."
試運行是工程層面的驗證；確認是法規層面的驗證 — 兩者都是必要的，互不取代。
5.1

Scope of Commissioning / 試運行範疇

Standard catalogue systems vs. site-built systems — documentation expectations

Original Text (ISPE 2016, pp.19–20)

5.1 Scope of the Commissioning

The commissioning process should be a well-planned, documented, and managed engineering approach to the start-up and turnover of both the system and the equipment to the End User. Commissioning should result in a safe and functional environment that meets established design requirements and stakeholder expectations (see also the ISPE Baseline® Guide: Commissioning and Qualification). The complexity of commissioning can vary, depending on the type of system.

If a risk-based approach is being used, the commissioning documentation may be used to provide evidence of the installation and operation. The commissioning documentation needs to be of an acceptable standard. Typical expectations for the commissioning documentation are provided (see Section 6).

5.1.1 Standard "Catalogue" Systems

Standard "Catalogue" Systems are comprised of mechanical components assembled and/or produced by a manufacturer for general industry applications. There is a limited standard menu of options with respect to hardware and/or software. A manufacturer normally provides a standard operations manual that applies to the operation and maintenance of the system. Standard "Catalogue" Systems are usually set to work following the manufacturer's instructions. Examples include freestanding freezers and refrigerators.

Commissioning is usually simpler for standard catalogue equipment, as the control system is an integrated part of the standard catalogue system, with data on all the components contained within the supplier documentation. A typical commissioning approach could follow the steps listed below:

  • Recording of system data
  • Verification of correct installation (installation verification)
  • Confirmation of satisfactory operation / temperature mapping (operational verification)

Generally, Standard "Catalogue" Systems have been set up in a factory by the manufacturer; typically, the scope of work does not include mapping — this is usually added to the vendor's requirements.

5.1.2 Site (Custom) Built Systems

Site (Custom) Built Systems normally require additional verification to ensure that operation is as specified, usually with more adjustment (set up and tuning) of the refrigeration and associated control systems, in order to ensure that performance meets the user requirements and design specifications.

解析與 CDMO 情境應用

試運行的核心定義

試運行（Commissioning）是在正式安裝（IQ）之前或同步進行的工程性驗證活動，目的是確認設備安全、功能正常、符合設計要求，並完成移交給最終使用者（End User）的過程。

ISPE 強調：試運行是「橋樑」— 連接安裝完成與正式確認啟動。沒有完善的試運行，確認活動的基礎就不穩固。

比喻：新屋交屋驗收

試運行就像房屋交屋前的驗收過程：建商帶你走遍每個房間，確認電燈會亮、水龍頭有水、門窗可以關緊。這不是政府驗屋（確認），但是交屋的工程前提。沒通過驗屋，建商不能交屋；沒通過試運行，GMP 確認不能開始。

風險基礎方式下的試運行文件

ISPE 允許以風險基礎方式使用試運行文件來支持確認活動（即「leveraging」或「bridging」策略）。這意味著：

  • 廠商提供的 FAT 數據可作為 IQ 的部分證據
  • 試運行中的功能測試可支持 OQ 的設計
  • 但文件必須達到 GMP 可接受標準（可追溯、可核查、符合數據完整性要求）
  • 需要正式的文件審查和批准流程，不能只是工程報告

練習思考

  1. 一台新購入的 -80°C 冷凍庫（標準目錄設備），廠商提供完整的 FAT 報告。您如何利用這份報告減少現場 IQ 的工作量？需要確認哪些條件？
  2. 如果試運行文件要達到「可接受標準」，具體指的是哪些 GMP 文件要求？（提示：數據完整性 ALCOA+）
  3. 現場客製建置的冷藏室，試運行調校（tuning）階段發現溫度均一性不佳。應如何記錄這個過程，以確保後續確認不受影響？
5.2

Commissioning Strategy / 試運行策略

Commissioning Plan objectives, roles, and acceptance criteria definition

Original Text (ISPE 2016, pp.20–22)

5.2.1 Execution Process

The testing strategy and the acceptance criteria should be documented in a Commissioning Plan prior to test execution. The objective is to:

  • Show that the work will meet Owner and regulatory agency expectations
  • Provide clear and early definition of deliverables and handover requirements
  • Define roles and responsibilities
  • Define the Engineering Change Management System
  • Define the approach to be used for training of the maintenance department and End Users
  • Ensure consistency of approach and testing across the project
  • Ensure full transparency on progress metrics (test execution and productivity)
  • Scope the testing required
  • Provide review and approval of test method statements
  • Provide progress reporting
  • Provide reporting and handling of test discrepancies
  • Define the location and marking (identification) of mapping points
  • Define the acceptance criteria / expected results
  • Witnessing requirements and notification procedures
  • Handling/retention of raw data
  • Format and content of the commissioning report
  • Defined responsibilities for operating and maintaining a facility during commissioning
  • Identify who is responsible for maintaining the operating log from start-up to handover
  • Define how handover is to be managed

The Commissioning Plan should also define how safety is considered. When executing the plan, Commissioning and Qualification may be performed in two distinct phases, or the phases can be combined.

Note: acceptance criteria are "non-negotiable" test results; expected results may be acceptable across a broader range, or are results taken for reference purposes.

5.2.2 Roles and Coordination

Typical roles and responsibilities of parties involved include:

  • Commissioning Lead — responsible for coordinating and managing commissioning activities and allocating resources; writes and/or executes the activity; responsible for accuracy of content
  • System Owner — reviews content; by signing the Plan and Test Report, agrees to the content; has decision making authority and is accountable for compliance to the URS; during construction, determines acceptance of the "as built" system at mechanical completion
  • Commissioning Team Member — involved in execution, documentation, and expertise (site activities: verification, safety analysis, protocol execution, punch items, maintenance training; office activities: document preparation, red-line updating, archiving)
  • Engineering/Technical Services and Validation Group — on distribution list; may review as SMEs but do not take direct action on commissioning documents
解析與 CDMO 情境應用

試運行計畫（Commissioning Plan）的核心功能

Commissioning Plan 是試運行的「憲法」— 在任何測試執行之前必須完成並批准。它的存在確保：

  • 所有相關方事前同意測試範圍和驗收標準
  • 沒有人可以在測試後才「倒填」標準（防止數據操縱）
  • 測試差異（discrepancy）的處理方式已預先定義
  • 資料保留和移交格式已明確規定

關鍵區別：驗收標準 vs. 預期結果

理解此區別對於稽查應對至關重要：稽查員會問「你的驗收標準是測試前定義的嗎？」

CDMO 中的角色對應

在 CDMO 環境中，試運行角色通常由以下部門承擔：

  • Commissioning Lead：工程/設施部門主管或專案經理
  • System Owner：QA 或生產部門代表（對法規合規負責）
  • Commissioning Team Member：工程師、儀控技術員、廠商代表
  • Validation Group：負責確認協議，可審查試運行文件作為 IQ 依據

System Owner 的角色特別重要：他/她在簽署試運行計畫時，正式接受對 URS 合規性的問責。

練習思考

  1. 試運行計畫中的「原始數據保留」條款，與 21 CFR Part 11 的數據完整性要求有何關聯？如果試運行數據只有紙本，應如何管理？
  2. System Owner 在試運行中「接受 as-built 系統」這個動作，對後續確認的 IQ 階段有什麼意義？是否可以省略？
  3. 如果試運行期間測試失敗，但技術人員直接修正後重新測試，未更新試運行計畫。這在稽查中會引發什麼問題？
5.3

Commissioning at the Design Phase / 設計階段的試運行活動

Design Review, FMEA risk assessment, URS verification, utility interactions

Original Text (ISPE 2016, pp.22–23)

5.3.1 The Design Review

From the commissioning perspective, the Design Review is intended for the commissioning team to become familiar with the project and to verify that the design has adequate provision for the tests required, as defined in the equipment specification and URS.

Requirements in the URS should be clarified with attendees. Key design documents should then be reviewed. Issues relevant to continuous operation of the Chamber are critical aspects to consider and include:

  • Chamber loading scenarios
  • Loading and unloading of products
  • External/adjacent environmental conditions

Typical documents for verification include:

  • Layout and HVAC zoning layout
  • Room environmental parameter schedule
  • Piping and Instrumentation Diagram (P&ID)
  • Functional specifications

During the Design Review phase, documents relevant to the areas surrounding the chamber and to the utilities serving it (e.g., hot water, chilled/glycol water, electricity) should be included in the review in order to properly understand the interaction between the Controlled Temperature Chamber and the rest of the facility.

The Commissioning Team should define the list and sequence of at-site activities and verifications needed, and complete the Commissioning Plan. A tailored approach is usually required as the sequence and activities are dependent upon the specific site conditions, utilities available, operating conditions and type of Controlled Temperature Chamber.

In this phase, the Commissioning Team should be given opportunity to provide suggestions to the designer, in order to obtain a design that will facilitate Commissioning Tests and activities. Suggestions may include availability of access to regulation points, provision of testing points in an appropriate location, or access ports to the room for installation of cabling, if required during temperature mapping.

5.3.2 Design Risk Assessment

A risk assessment may be used to help critique and develop a robust design. A Failure Mode Effects Analysis (FMEA) risk assessment can be used to identify possible failures that could lead to the loss of the required performance, identified by review of design and vendor documentation.

Risks should be evaluated as to their probability and severity, in order to determine the impact to process variation and effect.

Unacceptable risks should be mitigated following the preferred hierarchy of:

  • Elimination by design
  • Elimination by automated control
  • Elimination by procedural controls

The risk management requirements identified should be designated as critical and include all components, functions, and features of the design that serve to control risks. These functions and features should be tested during commissioning.

解析與 CDMO 情境應用

設計審查中試運行團隊的角色

試運行團隊參與設計審查的目的，不是批准設計，而是確保設計「可測試」。常見的試運行可測試性問題：

  • 感測器安裝位置沒有足夠的接線導管，mapping 時無法佈線
  • 冷藏室牆壁沒有預留穿線孔，臨時開孔影響氣密性測試
  • 壓縮機組沒有壓力測試連接點，預防性維護困難
  • 控制閥沒有旁通管路，維修時必須停機

在設計階段提出這些問題，成本遠低於施工後修改。

P&ID 在 CTC 試運行的核心作用

管線儀表圖（P&ID）是試運行最重要的設計文件之一，記錄：

  • 所有管線、閥件、感測器的位置和識別號
  • 儀控系統的連接邏輯
  • 壓力/溫度安全裝置的設定值
  • 公用設施（冷凍水、電力、壓縮空氣）的供應點

試運行完成後，P&ID 必須更新為「紅線版本」（as-built），反映所有施工期間的變更。這份文件最終成為設施生命週期管理的基礎。

FMEA 在 CTC 設計階段的應用

針對 CTC 設計的 FMEA 常見失效模式包括：

FMEA 識別的關鍵功能，必須在試運行時進行測試。

練習思考

  1. 一台步入式冷藏室計畫安裝在廚房旁邊（鄰近熱源）。在設計審查中，試運行團隊應提出哪些具體問題？
  2. 設計審查發現 P&ID 上缺少壓力安全閥的識別號。這個發現應如何記錄和追蹤？
  3. FMEA 評估後，壓縮機故障被列為高風險。如果決定用「程序控制」（定期巡檢）作為緩解措施而非增設備援，這在 GMP 合規上是否可接受？
5.4

Commissioning During Installation / 安裝階段試運行活動

Physical inspection, safety checks, setting to work, functional testing, red-line drawings, FAT/SAT

Original Text (ISPE 2016, pp.23–26)

5.4 Commissioning Activities during the Installation Phase

Commissioning activities may be divided into four broad categories:

  1. Inspection of the physical installation — field verification of installation drawings and documentation/test verification (e.g., pipework pressure and evacuation tests) to ensure compliance with design specifications
  2. Pre-operational safety checks
  3. Setting to Work — setting a static system into motion ("shake down") and regulation and adjustment
  4. Functional testing — regulation, adjustment, and functional testing may be iterative activities within fine tuning of the system

5.4.1 Inspection of the Physical Installation

The Commissioning Team scope should include confirmation that:

  • The equipment and materials are checked to ensure compliance with design data sheet and specifications
  • Installation has been completed in accordance with the design specifications and manufacturer instructions
  • As-built documentation is available and correct

Usually, 100% of the installation is verified (packaged units such as the compressor would be considered as a single system component).

It is usually a duty of the Commissioning Team to maintain a "red line" copy of the construction record documents. Comments and changes should be marked on the document following a defined procedure, to be turned over to the responsible party for updating the record documents to be provided to the System Owner.

Some of these activities may be performed at the vendor's factory and documented within specific Factory Acceptance Test (FAT) protocols/reports. Completion of this stage should verify that the installation meets specifications.

5.4.2 Pre-operational Safety Checks

This phase is intended to eliminate as many risks as possible in regard to the safety of personnel during commissioning and also during operation. The "Lock Out/Tag Out" procedure can determine that utilities (chilled water/gas/steam and electrical power) are provided to the system once the following are available and documented:

  • Conformity of electrical system and correct settings (e.g., overloads/fuse ratings)
  • Evidence of pressure test of utilities lines
  • Presence of pressure/temperature safety release devices (with right settings)

5.4.3 Setting to Work

This is the initial startup and tuning of the system. This may include:

  • Energizing the system
  • Filling with fluids
  • Check motor drives (mechanically, electrically) and direction of rotation checks
  • Internal layout of the Chamber verification and as-built dimension measurements
  • Chamber and doors tightness verification
  • Input/Output (I/O) check of the control system
  • Alarms check
  • Calibration of the instruments
  • Balancing and fine tuning

5.4.4 Functional Testing

Checks performed in previous phases should have been executed successfully as a prerequisite to functional tests. The system should be tested to confirm that the design performance is achieved within the acceptance ranges specified in all working modes.

Where feasible, the worst case conditions for the surrounding environment should be simulated during testing. Where the area being tested has duty/standby conditioning units, these should both be tested to ensure they will perform adequately. Studies of trends of the transition phase between the stop of the main system and the full operation of the standby system should be included in testing.

The operation and influence of the surrounding environment on defrosting systems should be verified and documented during the Commissioning and Qualification Phase.

5.4.5 Engineering Change Management

During Design — cumulative changes should not influence the ability of the design to meet user requirements. During Construction and Commissioning — changes proposed should be agreed with by the engineer of record. If a test fails and can be repeated after adjustments, it is acceptable to annotate the test sheet with the adjustments made and repeat the test; where changes are required, an engineering change control should be used to gain approval prior to execution and repeating the tests.

Once Qualification is complete, change should be managed through the site GMP change control system.

解析與 CDMO 情境應用

「紅線圖」(Red-Line Drawings) 詳解

紅線圖是施工期間所有設計變更的即時文件記錄。名稱來自傳統上用紅筆在藍圖上標注變更的做法。其重要性在於：

  • 記錄「as-built」狀態：實際安裝如何不同於設計圖
  • 任何未記錄在紅線圖的變更，在稽查中都是違規（未授權變更）
  • 紅線圖由試運行團隊即時維護，不是事後補寫
  • 完成後需正式轉為更新版本的工程圖，不能永遠停留在「紅線」狀態
「如果它不在紅線圖上，它等於沒發生。如果它發生了但不在紅線圖上，它就是未經授權的變更。」

工程變更管理：試運行期間的實務操作

試運行期間測試失敗是正常的 — 但處理方式決定文件的可接受性：

練習思考

  1. FAT 在廠商工廠中完成，但設備運輸到現場後發現壓縮機有輕微損傷。哪些 FAT 測試需要在現場 SAT 中重新執行？判斷標準是什麼？
  2. 試運行期間調校（Balancing and fine tuning）發現溫度均一性不符合設計規格。如果技術員直接調整 PLC 設定後重測通過，但沒有走工程變更流程，後續 IQ 審查時會面臨什麼問題？
  3. Lock Out/Tag Out (LOTO) 程序主要針對人員安全。但若 LOTO 記錄不完整，這對 GMP 合規有何影響（提示：想想設備使用狀態記錄）？
5.5–5.6

Handover, System Manual & Safety / 移交、系統手冊與安全

Punch list management, handover certificate, job safety analysis

Original Text (ISPE 2016, pp.26–27)

5.5 Handover, the System Manual, and Training

Handover usually represents turnover of the system to the user, with handover of operation and maintenance. Commissioning and Qualification activities are usually completed. There should be a documented record confirming that the functionality and operation of the system is considered acceptable and Commissioning can be considered complete. This may be the Commissioning or Qualification Summary Report, or a separate handover certificate, depending on site practices.

A punch list (snag list) is typically used to manage completion of the system to meet the specifications. Major items on this list would prohibit handover, other items that can be resolved following handover are generally accepted. Typical categories used for a punch list include:

  1. Items that affect performance — to be addressed prior to handover
  2. Items that affect safe operation of the equipment — to be addressed prior to handover
  3. Items that block next activities/verifications — to be addressed prior to handover
  4. Minor items that do not impact operation — to be addressed after handover
  5. Desirable changes/improvements — to be addressed after handover through the change control system

Following handover, responsibility for operation and maintenance of the system should be transferred to End Users and the maintenance team. Appropriate operation and maintenance procedures should be established.

5.6 Safety

A job safety analysis covering all the phases of commissioning should be prepared by the personnel who will execute the site activities. The analysis should describe the potential risks, their probability, and should identify protection devices. Operators or technical personnel should be informed about the outcome of this analysis when receiving permission to execute commissioning activities. When judged appropriate, the testing area or room should have signs informing personnel of risks or forbidding access.

解析與 CDMO 情境應用

Punch List（待辦清單）的 GMP 實務意義

Punch list 是試運行移交的關鍵工具，但其分類直接決定移交是否可以進行：

稽查員常關注：第 1-3 類項目是否在移交前確實完成關閉？若移交時仍有 open items 且屬 1-3 類，這是嚴重缺失。

移交後的責任轉移

移交（Handover）是一個正式的責任轉移事件：

  • 移交前：設施/工程部門對設備負責，GMP 尚未適用
  • 移交後：生產/QA 部門接管，GMP 完全適用
  • 操作 SOP、維護程序需在移交前建立並培訓相關人員
  • 移交後的任何變更必須走正式 GMP 變更管控，不能再以「試運行調整」處理

練習思考

  1. 試運行的 Punch list 中有 3 個第 4 類（輕微不影響操作）項目仍 open，確認工作是否可以開始？請說明理由和需要的文件記錄。
  2. 一台已完成確認的 -80°C 冷凍庫，因夏季空調故障導致設備間溫度升高 8°C 達 4 小時，之後恢復正常。需要執行哪些評估和記錄？是否需要重新確認？
  3. 客戶要求在已確認的冷藏室中增加一層貨架以提高儲存量。依據變更觸發矩陣，應走什麼程序？需要的最低限度重新確認是什麼？
Ref

Commissioning vs. IQ / OQ / PQ — Full Comparison

試運行 vs. 安裝確認 / 操作確認 / 性能確認 全面比較

"Commissioning is the engineering proof; qualification is the regulatory proof — both are necessary, they are not redundant."
試運行是工程層面的驗證；確認是法規層面的驗證 — 兩者都是必要的，互不取代。

The following table compares commissioning with the three stages of formal qualification. Understanding these differences — and where they overlap — is essential for designing an efficient, compliant qualification strategy for CTCs.

下表比較試運行與三個正式確認階段。理解兩者的差異與重疊，是設計高效合規的 CTC 確認策略的基礎。

校正追溯鏈說明 — Calibration Traceability Chain

Mapping 前的感測器校正必須建立完整的計量追溯鏈，確保測量結果可追溯至國家/國際標準：

NIST / SI 國際標準
↓
認可校正實驗室參考標準（ISO/IEC 17025）
↓
廠內工作標準（每年校正）
↓
Mapping 用溫度感測器（每次使用前校正）
↓
設備內建控制探針 / 獨立監控感測器

每個環節都必須有有效的校正證書，記錄：校正日期、有效期、不確定度、校正機構認可資格。校正記錄必須在 mapping 開始前完成，並包含在 mapping 報告的附件中。

比喻：試運行與確認的完美比喻

試運行 = 廚師烹飪時的試味
主廚烹飪過程中不斷嚐味、調整鹽糖、確認火候。這是廚藝的工程驗證——確保菜可以端出去。

確認 = 餐廳衛生稽查
政府衛生人員按照法規標準進行稽查，確認廚房設施、溫度記錄、衛生標準都符合要求。這不是在重複廚師的工作——它是獨立的法規驗證，給公眾（和監管機構）信心。

廚師的試味（試運行）讓衛生稽查（確認）更容易通過，但兩者不能互相取代：試味通過不等於衛生稽查過關，衛生稽查也不能替代廚師的烹飪技術。

核心訊息：完善的試運行讓確認工作更順暢、更有效率，但不能被確認所取代，也不能替代確認。兩者在 GMP 生命週期中各自有其不可取代的位置。

綜合練習：整合思考題

  1. 一個新建的 CDMO 設施計畫安裝 3 台 -80°C 冷凍庫、2 台步入式冷藏室和 4 台穩定性腔體。請描述如何設計一個整合的試運行與確認策略，以最大化效率、最小化重複工作，同時符合 GMP 要求。
  2. 客戶審計員詢問：「您的試運行文件和 IQ 文件有什麼不同？可以給我看紅線圖嗎？」請準備一個 2 分鐘的口頭解釋，說明兩者的角色和關係。
  3. 假設您是一個新設 CDMO 的 QA 主管，試運行負責人（工程部門）告訴您：「試運行都做完了，我們可以直接進行 OQ，跳過 IQ 嗎？因為試運行報告裡已經有所有的安裝核查數據。」您如何回應？需要什麼條件才能接受這個提議？
  4. Mapping 前的感測器校正需要 NIST 追溯性。您的廠內有一台未經 ISO/IEC 17025 認可的溫度校正器。這台設備能否用於 mapping 前的校正？如果不能，應如何解決？

Chapter 2: Testing Strategy

Chapter 6: Testing Strategy | 測試策略

ISPE Good Practice Guide: Controlled Temperature Chamber Mapping and Monitoring (2016)
Source Pages: 28–35  |  Section 02 of ISPE-CTC
Chapter Key Message / 章節核心訊息 A mapping study that only tests ideal conditions gives you a false sense of security — the risk lives in the extremes you haven't tested.
只在理想條件下進行的溫度分佈研究，只會帶給你虛假的安全感。真正的風險，藏在那些你從未測試過的極端條件裡。

Chapter 6 Contents | 本章目錄

Learning Objectives | 學習目標 6.1 Outcomes | 測試目標 6.2 Risk Assessment | 風險評估 6.2.1 Risk-based Approach | 風險導向 6.3 When to Map | 何時執行 6.3.1 Pre-mapping Requirements | 前置要求 6.4 Mapping Strategy Factors | 影響因素 6.4.1 Equipment Selection | 設備選擇 6.4.2 Sensor Number & Location | 感測器數量與位置 Sensor Placement Table | 感測器位置表 Test Condition Matrix | 測試條件矩陣 Risk Assessment Matrix | 風險評估矩陣

Learning Objectives | 學習目標

After reading this chapter, you will be able to:
  1. State the two primary outcomes that temperature mapping must confirm
  2. List the five major risk factors evaluated before developing a mapping strategy
  3. Explain why CFD modeling supplements but cannot replace actual testing
  4. Describe the rationale for sensor placement at corners, doors, vents, and obstructions
  5. Apply sensor number guidance based on chamber volume (<2 m³ vs. <20 m³)
  6. Compare empty vs. loaded test conditions and explain which represents worst-case
  7. Define measurement uncertainty and explain how calibration accuracy affects acceptance criteria
  8. Explain when seasonal variation (summer) represents the critical mapping period
  9. Describe minimum pre-mapping documentation requirements
  10. Apply zoning concepts for multi-unit HVAC systems
讀完本章後，你將能夠：
  1. 說明溫度分佈研究必須確認的兩大主要目標
  2. 列舉制定測試策略前需評估的五大風險因素
  3. 解釋為何CFD模擬只能補充、不能取代實際測試
  4. 描述感測器應放置於角落、門口、風口及障礙物旁的原因
  5. 依據腔體體積（<2 m³ 及 <20 m³）應用感測器數量指引
  6. 比較空載與滿載測試條件，說明哪種情境代表最壞情況
  7. 定義量測不確定度，並解釋校準精度如何影響接受標準
  8. 說明季節變化（夏季）為何是關鍵的映射時機
  9. 描述啟動溫度分佈研究前的最低文件要求
  10. 應用分區概念於多機組HVAC系統
6.1

Outcomes | 測試目標

What temperature mapping is designed to confirm — Source pp. 28

6.1 Outcomes

Testing is intended to:

  1. Confirm that the space that will be used for storage remains within defined limits with respect to temperature uniformity and stability over time across usable space.
  2. Determine locations representing operating temperature extremes to establish the strategy for monitoring and alarming the space used for storage and/or processing.

The operational temperature limits should be defined, together with any allowable excursions (time periods, acceptable limits).

Why Two Outcomes, Not One?

Outcome 1 answers: "Does this chamber work uniformly?" Outcome 2 answers: "Where do I put my monitoring sensors permanently?" Both are required — you cannot claim compliance without addressing both.

中文解析 | Commentary

ISPE將溫度分佈研究的目的簡化為兩個核心問題：

目標一：溫度均一性確認

確認整個可用儲存空間在整個使用期間，溫度維持在定義限度內。這是最基本的合規門檻。若某角落長期偏高2°C，但監測探針卻設在中央，你對偏差毫無預警。

目標二：確定極端位置 → 決定監測點

這是常被忽略但更具戰略意義的目標。分佈研究的最終產出，是一份科學化的監測點位選擇依據——最高點、最低點、最難維持溫度的位置，就是永久監測探針應該放的地方。

比喻：天氣觀測站的選點邏輯

你不會把氣象站設在最舒適的平地；你應該設在最容易出現極端天氣的山頂或海岸。溫度分佈研究的邏輯完全相同——找出極端，監測極端。

CDMO多客戶環境的意涵

在合約生產組織（CDMO）環境中，同一冷藏庫可能同時儲存多家客戶的產品，各自有不同的溫度規格（如2–8°C vs. 15–25°C）。Outcome 2的重要性更高：若監測點位選擇不當，無法保護最嚴格規格的客戶產品。

思考練習 1

問： 一間冷藏室的溫度分佈研究顯示，中央位置2–7°C，但東南角落持續9–10°C。這間冷藏室通過Outcome 1的測試了嗎？通過Outcome 2了嗎？

引導： 兩個目標各自獨立評估。未通過Outcome 1的設施，是否仍能使用？需要什麼條件？

思考練習 2

問： 你的永久監測探針放在腔體中央（最穩定的位置）。它能同時滿足Outcome 1和Outcome 2的要求嗎？為什麼？

6.2

Risk Assessment | 風險評估

Factors to evaluate before developing the test strategy — Source pp. 28–29

6.2 Risk Assessment

Prior to developing the test strategy, evaluate potential sources of excursions taking into account the following factors:

(Note: a company may use Computational Fluid Dynamics (CFD) modeling to evaluate impact of these factors but still needs some level of confirmation of the results through actual testing.)

  1. Purpose of the facility: storage, process cooling, transportation preconditioning
  2. Size: speed and magnitude of changes impacted by the footprint as well as the height, with attention to potential stratification with heights over 15 ft (457 cm)
  3. Layout/configuration: walls and obstructions, fixed racks, temporary racks, pallets on floors, duct supply and return locations
  4. Location of facility: geographic with respect to external climate exposures, physical location within temperature-controlled facility, windows, doors, traffic and access frequency
  5. Operating characteristics of the HVAC system: defrost cycles, redundant systems, number of units supporting storage space and how they interact with each other

CFD Modeling — Supplement, Not Substitute

CFD can help visualize airflow patterns and predict temperature gradients before physical testing. However, it cannot account for all real-world variables (door seals, product loading behavior, actual defrost timing). ISPE is explicit: actual testing is always required.

中文解析 | Commentary

ISPE要求在設計測試策略之前，先完成風險評估。這不是形式上的文件動作，而是決定你需要多少感測器、測試什麼條件的根本依據。

五大風險因素的實務意義

  • 用途（Purpose）： 純儲存 vs. 調溫（conditioning）的測試要求截然不同。調溫設備需要確認物品能在規定時間內達到目標溫度。
  • 尺寸（Size）： 15英尺（457公分）是溫度分層的警戒高度。超過此高度的倉庫，上下溫差可達3–5°C，必須在高低兩層各設感測器。
  • 佈局（Layout）： 固定貨架 vs. 移動棧板，直接影響氣流路徑。每次貨架配置改變，理論上都應評估是否需要重新分佈研究。
  • 地理位置（Location）： 面西的外牆在台灣夏季下午可能讓室內升溫超過1°C。
  • HVAC特性： 除霜週期（defrost cycle）是最常見的短暫溫度偏差來源，必須在測試設計中明確說明如何處理。

比喻：CFD就像天氣預報

天氣預報能告訴你明天可能下雨，但它不能取代實際的降雨量測量。CFD模擬能預測哪裡可能有熱點，但它不能取代真實的溫度分佈研究——因為真實世界總有模擬無法捕捉的變數。

風險評估矩陣：何時需要觸發分佈研究

思考練習 3

問： 你的CDMO設施新增一個大型冷凍乾燥機（lyophilizer），機器本身產生大量廢熱。這是否觸發相鄰冷藏室的重新分佈研究需求？依據ISPE的哪個風險因素判斷？

6.2.1

Risk-based Approach | 風險導向方法

ASTM-E2500 alignment and independent monitoring system rationale — Source pp. 29–30

6.2.1 Risk-based Approach

With the advent of ASTM-E2500 "Standard Guide for Specification, Design, and Verification of Pharmaceutical and Biopharmaceutical Manufacturing Systems and Equipment," an organization may use a risk-based approach, with the equipment installation and operation being verified. For further information, see:

  • The ISPE Good Practice Guide: Cold Chain Management
  • The ISPE Guide: Science and Risk-Based Approach for the Delivery of Facilities, Systems and Equipment

There should be a clear definition of the acceptance criteria; typically, this is provided in the URS or equivalent document.

Temperature mapping is used to confirm that the system is operating to meet specifications — i.e., the temperature range within the unit is acceptable.

It is standard practice in the pharmaceutical industry to provide monitoring of critical parameters using an independent system. Advantages include:

  • Calibration of the monitoring sensors can be carried out without impacting the system operation
  • The independent system becomes the quality "system of record"
  • The data can be used to provide continuous verification of acceptable system performance

Mapping results may be used to define the number and location of monitoring sensors for a warehouse, cold room, or chamber.

中文解析 | Commentary

ASTM-E2500 與風險導向驗證

ASTM-E2500將傳統的IQ/OQ/PQ驗證框架轉向「規格、設計、確認」的科學導向方法。關鍵轉變：不再強制要求固定格式的文件，而是要求有科學理由支持每個決策。對溫度分佈研究的實際影響是：你必須在協議書中解釋「為什麼選這些位置」，而不只是「我選了這些位置」。

獨立監測系統（Independent System）的三大優勢

  • 可獨立校準： 不影響系統正常運作即可校準監測探針。（試想：若監測系統與控制系統共用同一探針，校準時怎麼辦？）
  • 品質記錄系統（System of Record）： 監測系統的數據是官方記錄，不受設備控制系統的數據格式限制。
  • 持續驗證： 每一筆監測數據都是對「系統仍在規格內運作」的確認，形成連續的合規證據。

CDMO環境下的獨立監測系統設計重點

在多客戶CDMO設施中，獨立監測系統還必須滿足：

  • 數據存取控制（不同客戶只能看到自己的溫度記錄）
  • 21 CFR Part 11電子記錄合規（稽核軌跡、電子簽名）
  • 警報接收人分配（誰在哪間倉庫的偏差時收到警報）
  • 多套校準週期管理（不同設備可能有不同校準頻率要求）

思考練習 4

問： 你的冷藏設備控制系統（BMS）自帶溫度監測和警報功能。為什麼ISPE仍建議使用獨立的監測系統？這個建議在稽核時如何向查廠員解釋？

6.3

When to Perform Temperature Mapping | 何時執行溫度分佈研究

Timing within commissioning and relationship to supporting systems — Source pp. 30

6.3 When to Perform Temperature Mapping

Temperature mapping should start as early as possible during commissioning. This allows:

  • Early detection and resolution of any performance issues
  • Identification of potential operational constraints to discuss with End Users, to determine if the constraints are acceptable or require resolution

Where there are systems that support operation of a system (e.g., the warehouse, HVAC system, or a condenser water cooling system), these systems should be:

  • Identified and commissioned or in a known (and monitored) state prior to temperature mapping
  • This helps ensure complete and representative testing, and facilitates investigation in the event of performance problems

Acceptable Exception — Chilled Water System

It can be acceptable to temperature map an area served by an HVAC system where a chilled water system has not been fully balanced, IF the chilled water system is known to provide an adequate supply of chilled water at a constant temperature. The BMS/BAS could provide supporting data that the chilled water supply temperature remains within operating limits and that the HVAC cooling control valve does not fully open (indicating adequate supply).

中文解析 | Commentary

「盡早開始」的戰略意義

溫度分佈研究越早做，越容易在設計階段修正問題（成本低、影響小）。若等到設施完工後才發現一個角落有持續的熱點，此時可能需要大幅修改HVAC管路——工程代價遠超過一個早期測試的成本。

在台灣的CDMO環境，夏季的高溫高濕是最嚴苛的試驗條件。如果新設施在冬季完工並通過測試，應明確要求在夏季進行重複（seasonal）測試。

「前置系統就緒」的判斷基準

溫度分佈研究的結果，只代表「測試當時的系統狀態」。若測試時冷凍水系統處於非穩定狀態，測試數據可能無法代表正常操作條件。ISPE允許的例外條件很嚴格：

  • 冷凍水必須已知可提供穩定供應
  • 必須有BMS數據証明冷凍水溫度在範圍內
  • 控制閥未全開（証明冷凍水供應充足）

若這三個條件無法同時滿足，則分佈研究的測試數據不具代表性，必須在前置系統穩定後重新執行。

比喻：季節測試的重要性（台灣觀點）

台灣的夏季（7–9月）平均室外溫度35°C+，且濕度超過80%。冷藏設備的壓縮機效率在高溫環境下會下降（因為散熱條件變差）。一間在3月通過測試的冷藏室，到了8月可能出現以前從未出現過的溫度異常。這就是「季節最壞情況（summer worst-case）」測試的必要性。

思考練習 5

問： 你的新冷藏倉庫在1月完工，同月完成溫度分佈研究並通過。客戶問你：「這份分佈研究報告足以支持全年的產品儲存嗎？」你如何回答？需要增加什麼測試計畫？

6.3.1

Prior to Temperature Mapping | 分佈研究前置要求

Documentation checklist and pre-approval requirements — Source pp. 30–31

6.3.1 Prior to Temperature Mapping

Before temperature mapping commences, the commissioning plan/temperature mapping strategy should be approved by the Quality Unit.

The level of detail, number of personnel, or number of suppliers involved can vary depending on the type of project.

Temperature mapping equipment should be calibrated.

Documents which should be available from the supplier/construction company (as applicable):

  • Control System I/O list
  • Control System Drawings (control panel layout, wiring diagram)
  • Equipment and instrument lists
  • Materials receiving and inspection reports/material certifications
  • Equipment receipt and/or installation verification records
  • Cable tests (continuity, insulation)
  • Grounding (earth) tests
  • Motor insulation "megger" and direction of rotation tests
  • Fuse and breaker ratings/overload settings
  • Control loop wiring checks
  • Piping leak (hydrostatic) and evacuation tests
  • Pipework cleaning/flushing records
  • Record of cleaning for ductwork
  • Ductwork and Air Handling Unit (AHU) leakage tests
  • Operation and Maintenance manuals
  • As-built drawings/specifications

The test requirements will depend on the type of system, and how critical performance is to the product and/or business. Project specifications should define documentation and test requirements.

中文解析 | Commentary

「品質部門核准」為何是前置條件

溫度分佈研究是一個正式的驗證活動（validation/qualification activity）。依照GMP規範，所有驗證協議必須在執行前獲得品質部門（QA）核准。原因：

  • 確保測試設計符合法規期望
  • 確保接受標準已預先定義（不是測完才決定要不要過）
  • 若測試失敗，有明確的偏差處理程序

若先執行測試、再補核准，這在FDA稽查中屬於重大發現（Major Observation）。

設備校準的量測不確定度實務指引

ISPE特別提到：溫度分佈研究設備必須校準。這不只是「有校準證書」就可以，關鍵是理解校準的不確定度（measurement uncertainty）如何影響接受標準：

  • 若接受標準是2–8°C（範圍6°C）
  • 若感測器準確度為 ±0.5°C
  • 則實際可被感測器可靠偵測的範圍是 2.5–7.5°C
  • 廉價資料記錄器若準確度只有 ±2°C，則6°C的範圍根本無法可靠評估

規則： 感測器準確度 ≤ 接受標準範圍的 1/6（工業常規）。

量測不確定度計算框架

接受標準範圍 = 上限 - 下限
            = 8°C - 2°C = 6°C

感測器準確度要求（建議）:
  ≤ 接受範圍 / 6
  = 6°C / 6 = ±1.0°C（最大允許）

較嚴格建議（ISPE範例）:
  ±0.5°C（可得出 3–7°C 的有效判斷範圍）

廉價資料記錄器（±2°C）:
  -> 不適用於此接受標準
  -> 若要使用，須重新定義接受標準
     或取得設備豁免的科學依據

思考練習 6

問： 你的供應商提供了一批分佈研究記錄器，規格書顯示準確度為 ±1.5°C。你的產品儲存規格是15–25°C（範圍10°C）。這批記錄器適用嗎？請用數字計算並說明判斷依據。

6.4

Factors Influencing the Mapping Strategy | 影響測試策略的因素

Comprehensive factor list including load state, probe types, and sampling rate — Source pp. 30–32

6.4 Factors Influencing the Mapping Strategy

  • Purpose: storage, processing, transportation, conditioning
  • Type of facility: general warehouse, CRT warehouse, cold storage, freezer, refrigerator, incubator, stability chamber
  • Size of facility: span (air change rates and flow patterns), height (potential stratification)
  • Number of conditioning units controlling environment
  • Layout/configuration: open space versus walls, racks, obstructions; fixed vs. variable racks; duct supply/return positions; variable obstructions (moveable pallets, racks)
  • Location: geographic impact of external climate conditions; physical relationship within facility (conditioned space, windows, doors, exposed walls, high traffic areas, frequency and duration of access)
  • Contents of facility: motors, coils, lights, people; exothermic/endothermic reactive substances; hot material being cooled within facility
  • HVAC operating characteristics: defrost cycles, redundancies, interactions between evaporators, Fan Coil Units (FCUs), Direct Expansion (DX) coils; failure modes; hysteresis and time lags
  • Empty versus Full state:
    • Testing using a simulation of fully loaded conditions should be performed
    • Testing with a partial load can be considered unnecessary (system tested at operating extremes)
    • Note: typically, chambers are tested empty
  • Probe types: accuracy, reliability, ease of use and calibration — all impact measurement uncertainty
  • Buffered probes:
    • May be used for monitoring if performance relationship to stored product is known
    • Should NOT be used as controlling probes
    • Should NOT be used for mapping (when goal is to see actual room temperatures)
  • Sample rate: at least once every 5 minutes; may need to be more frequent if temperature spikes anticipated (defrost, door openings)
  • Operational requirements: how long doors open, how many people, traffic patterns, equipment

中文解析 | Commentary

空載 vs. 滿載 vs. 部分負載：測試情境比較

緩衝探針（Buffered Probe）的用途限制

緩衝探針（通常是包裹在甘油或沙粒中的探針）用來模擬產品感受到的溫度，而不是空氣溫度。ISPE明確區分三種使用情境：

  • 可以用（OK）： 作為永久監測點，前提是已確認緩衝探針讀值與產品溫度的對應關係
  • 不可以用（No）： 作為設備控制探針（緩衝延遲會造成控制失準）
  • 不可以用（No）： 作為分佈研究探針（因為目標是量測真實空氣溫度，而非產品溫度）

採樣頻率的選擇邏輯

ISPE最低要求：每5分鐘一次。但對以下情境需提高頻率：

  • 除霜週期（defrost cycle）：每次除霜可能使溫度在2–5分鐘內上升3–10°C，5分鐘間隔可能漏掉峰值
  • 頻繁開門（如物流分類區）：每次開門可能造成短暫溫度偏差
  • 調溫腔體（conditioning chambers）：需要追蹤物品升降溫曲線

建議： 對2–8°C冷藏庫，採用每1–2分鐘一次的採樣頻率，以確保能捕捉除霜事件的完整溫度曲線。

思考練習 7

問： 你的5°C冷藏室設有自動除霜功能，每4小時觸發一次，持續約8分鐘。你的分佈研究採用5分鐘採樣間隔。這個設計有什麼潛在問題？你會如何修改測試協議？

思考練習 8

問： 一個CDMO客戶要求你在「貨架滿載（其他客戶產品佔據80%空間）但該客戶產品佔最後20%」的條件下，特別執行一次分佈研究。根據ISPE的邏輯，這個要求合理嗎？如何用「部分負載通常不必要」的原則來回應？

6.4.1

Selection of Mapping Equipment | 量測設備的選擇

Accuracy requirements, measurement uncertainty, and humidity mapping — Source pp. 31–32

6.4.1 Selection of Mapping Equipment

Selection of the equipment to be used for mapping should consider the required accuracy and repeatability related to the predefined acceptance criteria.

Example: A unit with acceptance criteria of 2°C to 8°C (USP standard storage conditions). If the mapping system has an accuracy of ±0.5°C, this provides results (allowing for rounding) to meet the acceptance criteria of 2°C to 8°C.

The user requirements may have a tighter design specification, e.g., expected results of 3–7°C.

Important: Some low-cost mapping dataloggers have accuracy specifications of ±2°C. Use of these devices would not be appropriate for this application unless the acceptance criteria or expected results were revised to allow for the potential error.

Temperature sensors with a rapid response time are typically used for temperature mapping, to provide accurate information on system performance.

Humidity mapping considerations:

  • If humidity has been defined as a critical quality attribute, humidity sensors should be included
  • If there are no significant sources of humidity in the warehouse, it may be assumed that absolute humidity will equalize — a small number of sensors may suffice (one at low level, one at high level for stratification)
  • If there are significant sources of moisture, a greater number of humidity sensors will be required — number and location developed using similar concepts as temperature mapping
  • Where RH is the criteria, levels should be checked based on temperature variations using measured RH at the local temperature
  • Duplex sensors (T+RH combined) can simplify data analysis

Mapping sensor locations should be documented to allow a test to be repeated if necessary. The proposed load test strategy should be reviewed and approved by the Quality Unit and the System Owner.

中文解析 | Commentary

量測不確定度對接受標準的影響（實例）

情境一：標準冷藏（2–8°C）
  接受標準範圍 = 6°C
  感測器 ±0.5°C → 適用
  感測器 ±2.0°C → 不適用（±2°C超過範圍的1/3）

情境二：室溫儲存（15–25°C）
  接受標準範圍 = 10°C
  感測器 ±0.5°C → 非常適用
  感測器 ±2.0°C → 邊緣適用（需要額外評估）
  感測器 ±3.0°C → 不適用

情境三：超低溫（-80°C ± 10°C）
  接受標準範圍 = 20°C
  感測器 ±1.0°C → 適用
  感測器 ±3.0°C → 邊緣（需要評估）

結論：感測器準確度選擇標準
  感測器準確度 ≤ 接受標準範圍 × 1/4
  （保守：×1/6，非常嚴格：×1/10）

台灣CDMO設施的濕度管理考量

台灣夏季室外相對濕度常超過85%。對以下空間，濕度分佈研究尤其重要：

  • CRT倉庫（15–25°C）： 台灣夏季不開空調可能導致相對濕度超過60%，影響吸濕性藥品的穩定性
  • 冷凍/冷藏倉庫： 頻繁開門導致濕空氣進入，長期累積可能造成結霜，影響HVAC效能
  • 穩定性試驗箱（Stability chambers）： 同時監控溫度和濕度是基本要求（ICH Q1A）

比喻：快速響應探針 vs. 緩慢探針

用秒錶計時跑步，和用日曆計時跑步，你會選哪個？快速響應探針就像秒錶——能捕捉除霜事件、開門衝擊等短暫溫度變化。緩慢探針（或緩衝探針）就像日曆——只能告訴你大致趨勢，看不到關鍵的短暫偏差。

思考練習 9

問： 你正在為一個新的冷凍倉庫（-20°C ± 5°C）選擇分佈研究設備。供應商提供以下兩個選項：A款（准確度 ±0.3°C，$500/支），B款（準確度 ±1.5°C，$80/支）。你需要20個感測器。哪款符合ISPE要求？從成本效益角度如何說服管理層選擇合適的設備？

6.4.2

Sensor Number & Location | 感測器數量與位置

Science-based rationale, zone concepts, and the ISPE placement table — Source pp. 32–35

6.4.2 Determining Number and Locations for Mapping Sensors

The diagram in Figure 6.1 shows:

  • Small chambers (<70 cu ft / <2 m³): minimum suggested sensor locations as illustrated in the guide's left diagram
  • Medium chambers (<700 cu ft / <20 m³): minimum sensor locations as illustrated in the guide's right diagram

The inner box represents the working area (where product is stored); circles represent the sensor locations.

The sensor locations used for mapping should be defined based on:

  • Where product will be stored
  • The potential major influences on the internal conditions during use
  • The number and location of heating/cooling units
  • For conditioning units: sensors should be in the load
  • Defrost cycles should be considered when outlining test procedures

Critical Note on Rationale Requirement

General guidance should not be used without a supporting rationale. For example, "there should be a sensor every 4 m" — if the area being mapped has no factor that could cause a change in temperature, multiple sensors to monitor the same effects would be redundant. The rationale describing the location and number of sensors must be reviewed and approved by the Quality Unit and the area/System Owner.

Additional considerations for sensor number and locations:

  • Increase mapping sensor locations as necessary to monitor areas where changes in conditions are likely (e.g., near conditioned air discharge)
  • Where multiple HVAC outlets operate consistently, the area may be treated as a zone, with the mapping sensor layout developed for those zones
  • An area may be divided into zones that perform similarly — mapping a representative zone may provide adequate data to represent the whole area
  • Where appropriate, there should be a mapping sensor adjacent to the system control sensor

For systems with external walls: Data should be available on external conditions from another calibrated reference source (e.g., BMS/BAS) — not from the mapping system itself. This allows the designer to evaluate data in the context of design temperature ranges.

For conditioned rooms or standard catalogue systems: There should be data on facility/room conditions at the time of testing outside the store, to ensure that any open-door tests are representative of normal operating conditions.

中文解析 | Commentary

感測器位置決策流程

步驟1：確認腔體體積
↓
<2 m³：最少感測器（角、中央）約8–10個
<20 m³：最少感測器，增加高低層及每個角 約12–16個
>20 m³ / 倉庫：依分區邏輯設計，每區最少代表性點位
↓
步驟2：識別所有潛在影響因素
↓
有門 → 在門口兩側各加1個
有固定貨架 → 在最遠角落各加1個
高度>457cm → 在最高點額外加感測器
有障礙物 → 在死角區域各加1個
有HVAC出風口 → 在出風口附近加1個
↓
步驟3：確認是否有控制探針 → 旁邊加mapping探針
↓
步驟4：撰寫位置選擇科學理由（QA核准）
↓
步驟5：文件化座標圖，確保可重複執行

CDMO多客戶環境的分區（Zoning）策略

當CDMO設施有多個HVAC機組各自控制一個區域時，ISPE的分區概念特別實用：

  • 每個HVAC分區獨立評估： 兩個HVAC機組的交界處，是最可能出現溫度異常的位置（兩個控制系統的「無人管轄區域」）
  • 代表性區域可外推： 若西區和東區的佈局、負載完全相同，對西區的詳細分佈測試可以代表東區——但需要有充分的科學依據
  • 變動負載重新評估： 多客戶環境中，負載的組成和分佈可能每週都不同。需要評估「最不利的負載情境」並以此作為測試基準

Table 6.1 — Recommended Placement of Measuring Devices | 建議的量測設備放置位置

Test Condition Matrix | 測試條件矩陣

This matrix maps the intersection of load state, seasonal condition, and door scenario to clarify which combinations require testing. | 此矩陣說明負載狀態、季節條件與開門情境的組合，以釐清哪些組合需要測試。

Zoning Approach for Large Facilities

For areas with multiple HVAC units that operate consistently, each unit's area may be treated as a zone. Mapping a representative zone can provide adequate data to represent performance of the whole area — but only when the zones are truly equivalent in design, layout, and loading conditions.

When zones differ (e.g., one zone near an external wall, another in the building core), each must be mapped independently.

季節測試的台灣CDMO操作建議

根據ISPE的夏季最壞情況（summer worst-case）原則，台灣CDMO的建議做法：

  • 初始分佈研究（Initial Mapping）： 在7–9月（最熱季節）執行，以確保最惡劣環境條件下的合規性
  • 定期再驗證（Periodic Re-mapping）： 若初始研究在非夏季進行，應在設施首個夏季再執行一次
  • 台灣特殊挑戰： 颱風季節（7–10月）的氣壓變化可能影響密閉空間的換氣效率，是額外的環境因素
  • 記錄外部條件： 所有分佈研究報告應記錄測試當時的室外溫濕度（來自BMS或中央氣象局數據）

思考練習 10

問： 你的CDMO設施有三個2–8°C冷藏室，由三組獨立HVAC機組分別控制，佈局完全相同。你能否只對一個房間做完整分佈研究，然後以此代表另外兩間？根據ISPE的分區（zoning）原則，需要什麼前提條件？

思考練習 11

問： 一個FDA稽查員問你：「你的冷藏室感測器位置是如何決定的？」以下哪個回答最符合ISPE的科學化理由要求：

  1. 「我們依照行業慣例，每4平方公尺放一個。」
  2. 「我們參考了ISO 17025標準的最低感測器密度要求。」
  3. 「我們首先識別了所有可能影響溫度的因素（HVAC位置、門口、障礙物、高度差），然後在每個高風險位置放置感測器，並在協議書中逐一說明每個位置的選擇理由，由QA核准後執行。」

思考練習 12

問： 你的分佈研究報告顯示，冷藏室的最高溫點位於東北角（靠近外牆的上層貨架），測量值為7.8°C（接受標準上限8°C）。測試是在3月執行的，室外溫度22°C。這份報告是否足夠？如何向QA解釋夏季季節性風險？你會建議什麼後續行動？

★

Chapter 6 Summary & Key Takeaways | 章節總結與核心要點

Consolidated learning from all sub-sections

Chapter Key Message | 章節核心訊息 A mapping study that only tests ideal conditions gives you a false sense of security — the risk lives in the extremes you haven't tested.
只在理想條件下進行的溫度分佈研究，只會帶給你虛假的安全感。真正的風險，藏在那些你從未測試過的極端條件裡。

Core Principles Summary

  • Two outcomes required: Uniformity confirmation AND identification of monitoring locations — neither alone is sufficient.
  • Risk assessment first: The five factors (purpose, size, layout, location, HVAC) must be evaluated before designing the test strategy.
  • CFD supplements, never replaces: Computational modeling is a useful planning tool, but actual sensor data is always required by ISPE.
  • QA pre-approval is mandatory: The mapping protocol must be approved before execution — not after.
  • Equipment accuracy matters: Sensor accuracy must be appropriate for the acceptance criteria. Low-cost ±2°C loggers are often unsuitable for pharmaceutical applications.
  • Buffered probes ≠ mapping probes: Use unbuffered sensors during mapping to capture actual air temperatures, including short-duration excursions.
  • Sample at least every 5 minutes: Increase frequency when defrost cycles or frequent door openings are expected.
  • Test the extremes: Empty + full-load; summer worst-case; door-open scenarios — not just steady-state, not just empty.
  • Scientific rationale is non-negotiable: Every sensor location requires a documented reason, reviewed and approved by QA.
  • Seasonal variation is a risk: A winter test result does not guarantee summer performance — especially in Taiwan's climate.

CDMO多客戶環境核心要點

  • 目標二優先： 在多客戶環境中，永久監測點位的選擇尤為關鍵——必須能保護規格最嚴格的客戶產品。
  • 負載變化是持續性風險： 不同客戶產品的進出，使負載狀態持續變動。需定義「最不利負載情境」作為測試基準，並評估日常負載變動的影響。
  • 台灣夏季測試不可省略： 7–9月的夏季是最苛刻的測試條件。初始分佈研究若在低溫季節執行，必須規劃補充的夏季測試。
  • 獨立監測系統的多客戶設計： 數據存取控制、稽查軌跡、客戶隔離——這些是CDMO獨立監測系統的額外要求，超出ISPE基本要求。
  • 分區策略降低重新驗證成本： 合理的分區設計，讓局部改變只觸發受影響區域的重新評估，而非全場重新分佈研究。
  • 除霜週期文件化： CDMO設施的除霜事件必須在分佈研究中被完整捕捉和記錄，以向客戶和監管機構展示這些事件不構成產品風險。
  • 量測不確定度傳播： 校準不確定度 + 感測器準確度 + 數據採集系統誤差 = 整體系統不確定度。這必須在接受標準的設計中被考慮進去。

Chapter 6 Quick-Reference Summary Table | 快速參考總結表
