Learning Objectives / 學習目標

After studying this section, you should be able to… / 完成本節後，您應能夠…

English Objectives

  • Distinguish the scope and deliverables of IQ, OQ, and PQ for controlled temperature chambers (CTCs).
  • Explain the relationship between commissioning, FAT/SAT, and formal qualification under the ISPE risk-based approach.
  • Identify the types of temperature sensors (thermocouple, RTD, thermistor, chemical) and their accuracy characteristics.
  • Describe how worst-case mapping results drive the selection and placement of permanent monitoring probes.
  • Differentiate Engineering Alarms from Quality Alarms, and set Alert vs. Action alarm levels for a 2–8°C refrigerator.
  • Apply the thermal dampening fluid rationale, including justification requirements and fluid selection criteria.
  • List the mandatory and risk-based triggers that require scheduling a re-mapping study.
  • Explain how a continuous monitoring sensor strategy can substitute for periodic requalification mapping.
  • Apply ICH Q9/ISPE risk principles to determine re-mapping frequency for different CTC classes (standalone fridge, walk-in cold room, CRT warehouse).

中文學習目標

  • 區分受控溫度腔體（CTC）之 IQ、OQ、PQ 的範疇與交付成果。
  • 說明試車（Commissioning）、FAT/SAT 與正式確效在 ISPE 風險導向方法中的關係。
  • 辨識溫度感測器類型（熱電偶、RTD、熱敏電阻、化學型）及其精準度特性。
  • 描述最差情況測繪結果如何指導永久監測探針的選擇與安裝位置。
  • 區分工程警報與品質警報，並為 2–8°C 冷藏機設定警示（Alert）與行動（Alarm）警報值。
  • 應用熱阻尼液原理，包括論證文件要求與液體選擇標準。
  • 列出需要規劃重新測繪的強制性及風險導向觸發條件。
  • 說明持續監測感測器策略如何替代週期性再確效測繪。
  • 運用 ICH Q9/ISPE 風險原則，針對不同 CTC 類別（獨立冰箱、步入式冷房、CRT 倉庫）決定重新測繪頻率。
7

Chapter 7: Qualification / 第七章：確效

IQ · OQ · PQ  |  Commissioning relationship · Risk-based approach / 確效架構 · 試車關係 · 風險導向

7.0 When Is Qualification Required? / 何時需要確效？

Systems that have the potential to impact product quality require Qualification. This includes systems used to store GMP raw materials, intermediates, and finished products.

Where individual gel packs are verified before use (confirming system performance/adequate pack conditioning time), the systems used for their conditioning and storage may be categorised as engineering systems (i.e., commissioned systems).

The decision to Commission only versus Commission and Qualify is a judgment based on a comprehensive understanding of the product, process, and the nature of the system by appropriately qualified personnel. Refer to the ISPE Baseline® Guide: Commissioning and Qualification.

The traditional approach uses separate IQ and OQ protocols to provide documented evidence that installation and operation meet the user requirements/system specifications after commissioning. IQ and OQ may be combined into a single document.

Typically, a system Performance Qualification (PQ) is not required; any operational testing needed may be addressed within OQ. Where product-specific or loading-specific evidence is necessary, PQ is applied.

中文解說：確效的觸發條件

GMP 系統分類原則

ISPE 將受控溫度設備分為兩類：

  • 工程系統（Commissioned）：對產品品質影響間接，例如用於調節凝膠包溫度的冷房。試車（Commissioning）即可，不強制執行 IQ/OQ。
  • 確效系統（Qualified）：直接存放 GMP 原料、中間體或成品者。必須完成 IQ + OQ（PQ 視風險決定）。

類比：汽車出廠驗收 vs 年度保養

IQ = 新車交付時驗收（硬體規格符合訂單）；OQ = 試駕測試（操控在規格範圍內）；PQ = 實際載貨測試（滿載後性能達標）。試車（Commissioning）= 工廠組裝後的內部品管，為 IQ 提供基礎文件。

CDMO 現場提示

多產品 CDMO 中，同一台 2–8°C 冷藏箱可能同時存放生物製劑原液與成品。此類設備必須確效，且應在 PQ 中涵蓋代表性裝載配置，避免因產品切換導致溫度分布改變。

7.1 Installation Qualification (IQ) / 安裝確效

IQ should include:

  • A record of the major components — model numbers, serial numbers, supplier details
  • Confirmation that calibration has been conducted as required by the specifications
  • Confirmation that the specified utilities have been correctly connected — electrical supply, drainage, alarm cabling
  • Reference to the User Requirement Specification (URS) to confirm that the installed equipment matches the agreed specification
  • Listing of all critical instruments and their calibration due dates
  • As-built drawings or photographs showing equipment layout, probe locations, and utility connections

IQ may leverage commissioning documentation (FAT/SAT records, vendor certificates) provided the documents are referenced, controlled, and meet GMP traceability requirements.

IQ 活動表：CTC 安裝確效核心項目

重點提示

ISPE 允許 IQ 直接引用試車文件，但必須在 IQ 協議中明確交叉參考（cross-reference），並確認文件版本受控。不可僅口頭聲明「試車已完成」。

7.2 Operational Qualification (OQ) / 運行確效

OQ testing provides evidence that the system temperature ranges meet specifications during simulated operations. Key OQ requirements:

  • Empty chamber mapping — conducted for no less than 24 hours; sensors placed as defined in the test strategy; protocol must include a diagram showing sensor placement
  • Temperature study on the specified load — also no less than 24 hours
  • Open door testing (where applicable) — simulates routine access; results used to justify alarm delay settings
  • Power loss / temperature rise testing (where applicable) — how long until temperature exceedance after power failure
  • Quality-related alarm testing — confirm alert and action alarms trigger at set points
  • For liquid nitrogen or CO₂ freezers: confirm that the level of LN₂/CO₂ is maintained at set-point
  • Worst-case bracket approach: test at extreme conditions that cover all normal operating scenarios

OQ 活動表：CTC 運行確效核心測試

最差情況括號法 (Worst-Case Bracket Approach)

在 OQ 中，選取最不利的操作條件組合（例如：空腔 + 夏季環境 + 最高預期開門頻率），若在此條件下仍符合規格，則可覆蓋一般操作情境，無需逐一測試每種組合。

7.3 Performance Qualification (PQ) / 性能確效

For CTC systems, ISPE states that a system PQ is typically not required. Any operational testing required may be addressed in OQ. However, PQ may be warranted when:

  • Product-specific evidence is needed (e.g., temperature-sensitive biologics with narrow stability ranges)
  • Representative loading configurations must be demonstrated for multiple product types
  • Regulatory requirements or customer contracts explicitly call for PQ documentation
  • The system stores particularly high-value or critical intermediates where product loss risk is significant

Where PQ is conducted:

  • Use representative loading patterns — not necessarily full load, but covering the range of expected usage
  • Conduct loaded chamber mapping with thermal mass representative of actual product containers
  • Document the relationship between PQ results and the URS acceptance criteria
  • PQ protocols and reports follow the same GMP documentation structure as IQ/OQ

IQ / OQ / PQ 比較總表

7.4 Science and Risk-Based Approach / 科學與風險導向方法

ISPE promotes a science and risk-based approach to CTC qualification. The core concept is based on defining a test strategy and conducting testing once, with "Qualification" confirming that there is documented evidence that installation and operation meet specifications.

This documentation can be built through engineering commissioning documents, installation verification, and operational verification documented through commissioning / FAT / SAT. These activities become qualification evidence when they are:

  • Conducted per an approved protocol with pre-defined acceptance criteria
  • Reviewed and approved by Quality
  • Traceable and version-controlled
  • Cross-referenced explicitly in the IQ/OQ documents

Examples of the science-based approach are provided in Appendix 5 of the ISPE CTC Guide. The key principle: test once, document robustly, qualify efficiently.

Commissioning → Qualification 文件流程

FAT (Factory Acceptance Test)
↓
SAT (Site Acceptance Test)
↓
Commissioning (試車)
↓ leveraged / 引用
IQ + OQ (Qualification)
↓ (risk-based / 視風險)
PQ (if required)

CDMO 多產品應用要點

  • FAT/SAT 在設備供應商廠內完成，所有文件應以 CDMO 品質系統格式控制
  • 試車文件引用需在 IQ/OQ 協議中建立交叉參考索引（cross-reference index）
  • 多產品環境下，OQ 的裝載條件需涵蓋「最小裝載 + 最大裝載」兩種極端情況

📝 Practice Questions — Chapter 7 / 練習題

  1. A CDMO installs a new -20°C freezer for API storage. The vendor provides FAT records showing the unit maintained -20°C ± 3°C over 48 hours. Can these records directly serve as OQ evidence? What additional steps are needed?
    某 CDMO 安裝新的 -20°C API 冷凍庫，供應商提供 FAT 記錄顯示設備在 48 小時內維持 -20°C ± 3°C。這些記錄能否直接作為 OQ 依據？還需要哪些步驟？
  2. Why does the ISPE CTC Guide state that PQ is "typically not required" for temperature chambers, yet recommend it for high-value biologics storage?
    為何 ISPE CTC 指南表示冷藏設備「通常不需要 PQ」，卻又建議高價值生物製劑儲存應考慮 PQ？
  3. During OQ door-open testing, the chamber temperature exceeds the upper alarm limit within 4 minutes and recovers in 12 minutes. How should this result influence the alarm delay setting? Is this result a pass or fail?
    OQ 開門測試中，腔體溫度在 4 分鐘內超過警報上限，12 分鐘後恢復。此結果如何影響警報延遲設定？這算通過還是未通過？
8

Chapter 8: System Monitoring / 第八章：系統監測

Sensor types · Probe placement · Thermal dampening · Alert/Alarm strategy · 21 CFR Part 11 / 感測器類型 · 探針佈置 · 熱阻尼 · 警報策略 · 電子記錄要求

8.0 Independent Monitoring Principle / 獨立監測原則

It is considered good practice to use an independent system to monitor critical parameters. Calibration of monitoring probes can be performed without impacting system operation. The location of probes is determined during mapping.

Monitoring systems used in practice include:

  • Conventional chart recorders
  • Datalogging chart recorders
  • Building Management Systems (BMS) / Building Automation Systems (BAS)
  • Supervisory Control and Data Acquisition (SCADA) systems

The choice depends on the facility, the number of CTCs to monitor, and regulatory expectations. BMS systems used for GMP monitoring must comply with data integrity requirements, including audit trails and access control.

監測系統選型比較 & 21 CFR Part 11 適用性

21 CFR Part 11 BMS 最低要求 (FDA 電子記錄)

  • Audit trail：所有記錄的建立、修改、刪除均需留下追蹤記錄，含時間戳與操作者身份
  • Access control：依職能限制讀取與修改權限，具備唯一用戶ID
  • Data integrity：電子記錄不可被輕易刪改；需具備備份與災難復原機制
  • Electronic signatures：若用於正式 QC 記錄簽核，需符合電子簽名要求
  • Validation：BMS/SCADA 軟體需要 CSV（電腦化系統驗證）

8.1 Temperature Sensor Types / 溫度感測器類型

Three main types are used in GMP monitoring:

1. Thermocouples (熱電偶)
Operate via the Seebeck effect — a temperature gradient across a conductor generates a voltage. Two dissimilar metals form a circuit where the voltage difference is measurable (1–70 µV/°C for standard combinations). Cables and joints can be prone to damage. A common protocol allowance is up to 1% sensor failure without invalidating the test run, provided failed sensors are not in critical regions.

2. Resistance Temperature Detectors (RTDs) and Thermistors (熱電阻)
Based on resistance change with temperature. RTDs use metal (resistance increases with temperature); thermistors use ceramic material (resistance decreases with temperature). Measured using a Wheatstone bridge with a small current. High-quality RTDs may last >8 years in accelerated life tests. Wiring configurations (3-wire, 4-wire) minimise cable resistance effects.

RTD accuracy classes (IEC 751):

  • Class A: ± 0.15°C at 0°C (± 0.27°F at 32°F)
  • Class B: ± 0.30°C at 0°C (± 0.54°F at 32°F)

3. Chemical Indicators (化學型指示劑)
Chemicals that change colour with temperature. Used only to record minimum/maximum temperatures. Not considered accurate; no time record associated with temperature change. Not suitable for continuous GMP monitoring.

感測器精準度與選型指引

選型決策原則

對於 2–8°C 冷藏設備：

  • 接受範圍窄（僅 6°C 跨度），應選用 RTD Class A（±0.15°C），確保感測器精準度不佔用過多接受範圍餘裕
  • 熱電偶適合廣域測繪（±1.5°C 精度對 2–8°C 範圍仍屬偏大），需搭配高精度的參考傳感器進行現場校準
  • 化學型指示劑僅適用於貨物隨附的最低/最高溫度確認，不可用於設備確效或持續監測

8.2–8.3 Number and Location of Monitoring Probes / 探針數量與位置

Monitoring sensors should be placed where stored product will experience the maximum and minimum temperatures and, where applicable, more extreme humidity during normal CTC operation. At-risk (worst-case) locations are identified during mapping.

General sizing guidance:

  • For units <2 m³: one monitoring sensor in the worst-case location (typically the hottest location for a below-ambient unit) may be acceptable. A single sensor provides robust detection of operational or performance issues.
  • For larger systems or those with multiple cooling units: more sensors are justified to ensure adequate coverage of positions where stored product experiences maximum and minimum temperatures (and/or humidity).

Permanent sensor placement considerations:

  • Risk-based worst-case storage locations from mapping results
  • Single vs. dual temperature control unit placement
  • Volume of controlled space; density of materials and obstructions
  • High/low storage locations (warm air rises)
  • Independent heat sources (production equipment) within the CTC
  • Door areas and ingress/egress locations
  • Frequency of personnel and forklift ingress/egress during working hours
  • Operations outside working hours (lower traffic, different thermal dynamics)
  • Air conditioning of loading area — humidity and frost on evaporator coils
  • Sensors must not interfere with product movement or storage, and must be positioned in multiple geometric planes

The mapping results and data analysis are summarised in a report recommending optimum sensor locations for approval by the Quality Unit and System Owner.

探針佈置實務：CDMO 步入式冷房決策矩陣

比喻：監測探針就像保全攝影機

保全攝影機不是每個角落都裝一台，而是裝在「最有可能出問題」的位置：出入口、盲角、貴重物品旁。CTC 的監測探針邏輯相同——根據測繪找出風險位置，針對性佈置，而非均勻分布。

8.4 Thermal Dampening Fluids / 熱阻尼液

Monitoring probes may have alarm delay times or be placed in thermal dampening fluids to avoid nuisance alarms from short-term temperature variances due to loading/unloading.

Air Probes with time delays:

  • Delay times must be justified as having no product impact
  • Must consider the monitoring system sample frequency: if product has an acceptable excursion limit of 30 minutes and the system samples every 15 minutes, every alarm is potentially an OOS situation
  • Standard approach: alarm delay of 15 minutes is commonly used as a default for units with a wide range of operational loads

Probes in thermal dampening fluid:

  • The dampening fluid must simulate the storage of product in primary containers
  • The fluid must react to CTC temperature changes quicker than the primary container/packaging
  • Justification must consider: container size and material of construction; fluid selection (glycol, glycerin, Paratherm™); location of probe within the container
  • Probe must be suitable for immersion; procedures confirm correct liquid level and probe positioning
  • For a variety of containers, a conservative (worst-case smallest container) approach guides the probe medium design
  • Account for both primary containers and secondary packaging thermal mass

熱阻尼液 vs 時間延遲決策指引

15分鐘延遲設定的科學依據

ISPE 解釋 15 分鐘標準延遲的合理性：

  • 低溫設備開門後，密度較高的冷空氣會從腔體底部流出，被溫暖環境空氣取代，降溫需要時間
  • 統一延遲設定（15 min）可降低因設備個別設定不一致而導致的錯誤風險
  • 15 分鐘內的短暫溫升通常不代表系統異常，超過 15 分鐘則可能指向設備問題或人員忘關門
  • 警示：若產品穩定性限制（stability limit）接受時間 < 15 分鐘，此標準設定不適用，需客製化評估

8.5 Alarm Set Points / 警報設定值

Good practice is to define a clear alarm strategy for the CTC with two distinct categories:

8.5.1 Engineering Alarms (工程警報)

Generated by the temperature conditioning system and its control system. Include: system fault, high/low pressure, high/low temperature, temperature sensor fault (open/closed circuit). These require an engineering action.

Temperature alarm set points are defined based on system "as commissioned" performance — typically just outside the ± 3 standard deviation range to avoid nuisance alarms while ensuring early detection of potential problems.

Rationale: for a normal distribution, 99.7% of results lie within ±3σ. Using ±3σ set points creates very few false alarms while reliably detecting operational drift.

8.5.2 Quality Alarms (品質警報)

Alarms from the independent monitoring system, configured based on the defined temperature storage limits. Two levels are typically defined:

  • Alert (警示)：Tighter than the specification; triggers investigation. Typically ±1°C inside the specification band.
  • Action/Alarm (行動警報)：At or just inside the specification limits; triggers immediate action and investigation.

Example: For a 2–8°C unit with ±0.5°C sensor calibration accuracy:

  • Alert limits: 3°C and 7°C (37°F and 45°F)
  • Action limits: 2°C and 8°C (36°F and 46°F)

Alert vs Alarm 設定值範例：2–8°C 冷藏機

Engineering Alarm Set Point Calculation / 工程警報計算

Based on ≥24 hours of operational data at steady state:

Upper engineering alarm = Mean + 3σ
Lower engineering alarm = Mean − 3σ

Example: If the steady-state mean is 4.5°C and σ = 0.3°C:
Upper engineering alarm = 4.5 + 3(0.3) = 5.4°C
Lower engineering alarm = 4.5 − 3(0.3) = 3.6°C

This means engineering alarms are narrower than quality alerts, providing the earliest possible warning before product risk occurs.

📝 Practice Questions — Chapter 8 / 練習題

  1. A BMS monitoring system for a 2–8°C refrigerator has a 15-minute sampling interval. A product's stability data shows it can tolerate only a 20-minute excursion above 8°C. Is the 15-minute alarm delay still appropriate? Explain the risk and what should be done.
    BMS 系統每 15 分鐘採樣一次，但產品穩定性只允許 8°C 以上偏差不超過 20 分鐘。15 分鐘警報延遲是否仍適用？請說明風險並提出對策。
  2. Your walk-in cold room has a steady-state mean of 4.2°C and a standard deviation of 0.4°C. Calculate the engineering alarm set points and explain why they differ from the quality alert limits (3°C / 7°C).
    步入式冷房穩態平均為 4.2°C，標準差 0.4°C。請計算工程警報設定值，並說明為何與品質警示值（3°C / 7°C）不同。
  3. A probe is placed in a container of glycerin to simulate the thermal mass of a 10 mL vial. When is this approach appropriate, and what documentation must be generated?
    探針浸入甘油容器以模擬 10 mL 小瓶的熱質量。何種情況適合此方法？需要產生哪些文件？
  4. During an FDA inspection, the inspector asks why the BMS does not have an audit trail for temperature data modifications. What is the regulatory basis for this requirement, and what is the immediate corrective action?
    FDA 查廠時，查察員詢問為何 BMS 對溫度數據修改沒有審計追蹤記錄。此要求的法規依據是什麼？應立即採取哪些糾正措施？
9

Chapter 9: Periodic Evaluation & Frequency of Thermal Mapping Studies / 第九章：週期性評估與熱測繪頻率

Re-mapping triggers · Risk-based frequency · Continuous verification · Excursion documentation / 重新測繪觸發條件 · 風險導向頻率 · 持續驗證 · 偏差文件

9.0 Periodic Assessment Framework / 週期性評估框架

CTCs should be periodically assessed to determine the need for re-validation (re-mapping). Control systems, equipment, monitoring, and procedures should be part of this periodic evaluation to ensure the unit still operates in a verified/qualified manner.

The evaluation should include, but is not limited to, a review of:

  • Changes made to the system
  • Changes made to storage locations (rack/bin configuration)
  • Calibration history
  • Equipment use logs
  • Deviation investigations
  • Maintenance and repair history
  • Temperature mapping studies
  • Operational procedures
  • Existing verification/qualification documentation
  • Ambient temperature profiles (seasonal extremes)

Data collected from CTCs equipped with multiple permanently installed monitoring probes may be an acceptable substitute for requalification temperature mapping studies, provided the probes have a demonstrated history of successful operation including calibration and maintenance.

週期性評估 vs 重新測繪的決策邏輯

兩種不同的評估行動

Periodic assessment（週期性評估）：文件審查型——回顧校準記錄、警報歷史、SOP 變更、偏差、維護記錄。是每次週期性評估的最低要求，不一定觸發重新測繪。

Re-mapping（重新測繪）：實地測量型——重新在腔體中佈置溫度探針，運行 ≥24 小時，產生新的溫度分布數據。由 risk assessment 或觸發事件決定是否需要。

類比：健康檢查 vs 手術

週期性評估如同每年的健康檢查（血液報告、X 光），是例行性的。重新測繪如同精密外科手術前的術前評估——只有在有臨床指徵（觸發條件）時才執行，但頻率和指徵應提前在書面中定義清楚。

持續監測數據替代重新測繪的前提條件

  • 探針已安裝於測繪確定的最差情況位置
  • 探針具有完整的校準歷史（持續無 OOT / OOS）
  • 維護記錄完整，無未解釋的數據缺口
  • 監測系統本身已通過 CSV（電腦化系統驗證）
  • 替代方案需在 VMP（驗證主計畫）中明確定義

9.1 Re-mapping Triggers / 重新測繪觸發條件

Mapping exercises should be repeated according to risk assessment results or whenever significant modifications are made to the facility or temperature-controlling equipment.

System / Equipment triggers:

  • Equipment repair affecting temperature performance (e.g., compressor replacement, refrigerant recharge)
  • Relocation of the CTC to a different area
  • HVAC changes affecting the space surrounding the CTC
  • Changes to racking, bin configuration, or storage organisation patterns
  • Addition or removal of de-stratification fans
  • Changes to door configuration or door seals

Performance / Trend triggers:

  • Increasing frequency of temperature alerts or alarms (negative trend)
  • Temperature deviations outside specification
  • Seasonal extremes exceeding historical data range
  • Monitoring data showing increased variability or drift

Regulatory / Administrative triggers:

  • Regulatory inspection observations or internal audit findings
  • Number of SOP changes beyond a threshold defined in the VMP
  • Number of change controls to the area, temperature control system, or monitoring system
  • Scheduled requalification frequency defined in the VMP (e.g., every 3 years)

重新測繪觸發條件查核清單 (Re-mapping Trigger Checklist)

Mandatory = automatic re-mapping required  |  Risk-based = risk assessment determines need  |  Routine = per VMP schedule

9.2 Risk-Based Frequency / 風險導向頻率

A Risk Assessment is recommended to determine the frequency of periodic review and the need for repeating mapping. The frequency should be aligned with the site's Validation Master Plan (VMP) and based on risk factors including:

  • Local regulations and regulatory expectations for maintaining a validated state
  • Regulatory inspection observations and internal audit observations
  • History of performance in maintaining the desired temperature range
  • Number of temperature deviations (number of alerts and alarms)
  • Number of SOP changes
  • Number of change controls to the area, temperature control system, or monitoring system

Typical industry practice:

  • Remapping frequency: every 3 to 5 years — for standard storage units with stable performance history
  • Critical product storage: annually — for high-risk, temperature-sensitive, or high-value products
  • The rationale for the chosen frequency must be documented for the facility and/or equipment

Risk factors that increase frequency:

  • High exposure to environmental extremes (refrigerated storage directly exposed to seasonal fluctuations)
  • Narrow operating range (e.g., -20°C ± 5°C vs. 15–25°C)
  • High product value or supply-chain criticality
  • Old equipment with degrading performance history

The storage of high-value and/or temperature-sensitive products may warrant more frequent re-verification/re-qualification. Maintaining product availability in the supply chain is a critical quality and customer-focused consideration.

CDMO 多產品週期性評估決策矩陣

CRT 倉庫週期性維護 — 具體檢查內容 (ISPE 建議)

  • 建築外殼（牆體、門封、遮風簾）目視檢查，確認無明顯劣化
  • 回顧監測系統、HVAC 系統警報歷史，識別負面性能趨勢
  • 確認 HVAC 平衡風門仍在試車時的設定位置
  • 冷熱盤管清潔（如需要）
  • 確認控制閥非在 100% 開度運行（若是則代表系統正達到性能極限）

9.3 Continuous Performance Verification / 持續性能驗證

An alternative to periodic re-mapping: continuous performance verification using a sufficient number of permanently installed monitoring sensors. This strategy has become more feasible due to the reduced cost of radio transmitter sensors.

How it works:

  • Additional sensors are installed beyond the minimum monitoring requirement, placed at positions that would detect performance degradation from any direction (unit cooler failure, structural degradation, loading pattern changes)
  • Storage locations are formally defined and any revisions addressed through change control, allowing reassessment of probe number/location
  • The ongoing monitoring data provides continuous evidence that the system operates within specification

Design requirements for continuous verification:

  • The number and location of sensors must be determined based on ability to detect any impact of the conditioning system performance and system construction issues
  • Sensors must cover all zones where a degradation event would be detectable — including corners, near unit coolers, door areas, and stratification zones
  • For a walk-in unit in use, mapping may be performed with the unit loaded, using sensor locations from the initial mapping where possible

ISPE provides Figures 9.1–9.4 as examples of cold room sensor layout designs for both initial mapping (sparse sensors) and continuous verification (denser sensor arrays).

持續驗證策略 vs 週期性重新測繪比較

CDMO 持續驗證設計要點

對於多產品 CDMO 冷藏倉庫，持續驗證策略特別有價值：

  • 不同客戶產品的裝載模式各異，若每次換產品都要重新測繪，成本極高
  • 透過在最差情況位置安裝足夠密度的永久感測器，可覆蓋各種裝載場景
  • 每次裝載變化通過變更管制評估——若新裝載模式不改變最差情況位置，現有監測即可繼續
  • 關鍵：感測器陣列設計必須包含「能偵測到製冷機組性能下降」的位置

9.4 Handling Excursion Documentation / 偏差文件處理

A point person or department should be formally identified to coordinate the response to temperature excursions outside specified limits.

Excursion response protocol elements:

  • Immediate containment — assess whether product has been compromised; initiate product quarantine if needed
  • Root cause investigation — equipment failure, human error, systemic issue, or environmental factor
  • Impact assessment — review product's temperature stability data; determine if the excursion duration × magnitude is within the product's known stability budget
  • Deviation report — formal GMP documentation of the event, investigation, and disposition decision
  • CAPA (Corrective and Preventive Actions) — address root cause to prevent recurrence
  • Trend review — incorporate excursion data into the next periodic evaluation to assess whether re-mapping is warranted

Walk-in freezer / refrigerator specific checks (periodic maintenance):

  • Envelope inspection: door seals, moisture/ice buildup as indicator of air leakage
  • Alarm history review for negative performance trends
  • Verify refrigeration set point is being maintained (e.g., compressor suction pressure)
  • Confirm coils are cleaned, fan operation checked, control valves and thermal expansion valves verified, defrost settings and operation verified

溫度偏差回應流程（GMP 要求）

1. 即時遏制 (Immediate Containment)

確認警報真實性 → 隔離受影響產品 → 通知 QA 與倉庫負責人

↓
2. 根本原因調查 (Root Cause Investigation)

設備故障 / 人員操作 / 環境因素 / 系統性問題

↓
3. 產品影響評估 (Product Impact Assessment)

偏差持續時間 × 偏差幅度 vs. 產品穩定性預算（stability budget）

↓
4. 偏差報告 (Deviation Report)

正式 GMP 文件紀錄事件、調查結果、產品處置決定

↓
5. CAPA 預防再發 (Corrective & Preventive Action)

設備維修 / 程序修訂 / 人員培訓 / 監測升級

↓
6. 趨勢分析 → 週期性評估 (Trend → Periodic Evaluation)

偏差數據納入下次週期性評估，決定是否需要重新測繪

📝 Practice Questions — Chapter 9 / 練習題

  1. Your CDMO has a 2–8°C walk-in cold room storing three different client biologics. Client A requires annual re-mapping in their quality agreement; Client B and C have no specific requirement. How do you determine the overall re-mapping frequency? What document governs this decision?
    您的 CDMO 有一座 2–8°C 步入式冷房存放三個客戶的生物製劑。客戶 A 在品質協議中要求每年重新測繪；客戶 B 和 C 沒有特定要求。如何決定整體重新測繪頻率？哪份文件管理此決策？
  2. A walk-in cold room had its evaporator fan replaced six months after the last mapping study. Does this trigger a mandatory re-mapping? If not, what risk assessment questions must be answered?
    步入式冷房在最後一次測繪後六個月更換了蒸發風機。這是否觸發強制重新測繪？若否，需要回答哪些風險評估問題？
  3. A facility wants to adopt continuous monitoring (10 permanent sensors) as a substitute for periodic re-mapping of a -80°C ultra-low freezer storing cell therapy products. What are the minimum requirements for this approach to be accepted by FDA?
    某設施希望用 10 個永久感測器的持續監測方案替代 -80°C 超低溫冷凍庫的週期性重新測繪。此方法要獲得 FDA 接受，最低要求是什麼？
  4. During annual periodic review, you notice the cold room has had 12 temperature alerts in the past 12 months vs. 2 in the previous year. What actions does ISPE guidance recommend?
    年度週期性評估中，您發現冷房過去 12 個月有 12 次溫度警示，相較前一年僅 2 次。ISPE 指導建議採取哪些行動？
★

Core Message / 核心訊息

Integrating Chapters 7, 8, and 9 / 整合第七、八、九章

"Qualification proves a snapshot; monitoring proves the state over time — both are required to demonstrate ongoing control."

「確效證明的是某一時刻的快照；監測證明的是隨時間的持續狀態——兩者都是展示持續控制的必要條件。」

Why Both Are Required / 為何兩者缺一不可

Qualification (IQ/OQ/PQ) establishes that a CTC was installed correctly and did perform within specification under defined test conditions — typically a 24-hour or defined-duration snapshot. It answers the question: "Is this system capable?"

Continuous monitoring establishes that the system continues to perform within specification across every hour of every operational day, under real-world loading patterns, seasonal temperature swings, door-opening events, and equipment aging. It answers: "Is this system actually in control right now?"

Periodic evaluation bridges the two — it reviews monitoring data trends, maintenance history, and change history to determine whether the qualification status remains valid, or whether a new mapping study is needed to re-establish the snapshot.

In the ISPE framework, a CTC is considered to be in a state of control only when all three elements are in place:

  1. Valid, current qualification documentation (IQ + OQ)
  2. Functioning continuous monitoring with calibrated probes in worst-case locations
  3. Regular periodic evaluation with documented risk assessment for re-mapping decisions

三要素整合框架 / Three-Element Integration

CTC State of Control
受控溫度腔體之控制狀態
📂
Qualification

IQ + OQ
"Was it capable?"
確效文件

🔌
Monitoring

Probes + Alarms
"Is it in control now?"
持續監測

📈
Periodic Review

Risk assessment
"Is requalification needed?"
週期性評估

CDMO 視角總結

對於承接多客戶、多產品的 CDMO，這三要素構成了「溫控設備生命週期管理」的核心：

  • 確效：在設備安裝、重大變更後，用受控測試證明設備有能力達到規格
  • 監測：每天 24 小時、每週 7 天，持續確認設備仍在控制狀態，保護所有客戶的產品
  • 週期性評估：每年（或依 VMP 頻率）系統性回顧，識別性能劣化趨勢，決定是否需要重新測繪

缺少任何一環，GMP 合規性就不完整。

Chapter 10: Operational Issues | 操作問題

Section 10.1 — Challenging the Area with Operational Activities | 以操作活動挑戰受測區域

ISPE Source Text

10.1 Challenging the Area with Operational Activities

The area being mapped should be challenged with specific known operational activities during the thermal mapping process. These activities should simulate normal processes and functions that would occur for routine operations, such as opening interior doors, opening exterior doors (Receiving Dock Doors, Shipping Dock Doors), running of equipment (e.g., thermo-formers, stretch wrappers, forklifts, conveyors) etc. where there is a potential impact to the conditions.

By performing these functions and operating equipment during the execution of the mapping studies, cause and effect relationships can be identified for the thermal profile.

Operational activities to simulate during mapping include:

  • Opening interior and exterior doors (dock doors, personnel doors)
  • Running warehouse equipment: forklifts, conveyors, stretch wrappers
  • Simulating loading and unloading cycles
  • Normal personnel traffic through the space

Note on Cause and Effect

The primary purpose of operational challenges is to capture the actual thermal profile experienced during real production — not an idealized empty-room baseline. A mapping study that omits these activities may underestimate temperature variability and produce specifications that cannot be met during routine operation.

中文解析 & CDMO應用

操作挑戰與熱圖譜映射

核心概念：操作活動挑戰

熱映射研究不只是在空置、靜態的設備中放置感測器。ISPE要求在模擬真實生產條件下執行映射，以暴露潛在的溫度變化因子。

這等同於在「最接近實際使用場景」的條件下驗證設備性能。

CDMO共用冷藏室裝載風險場景

在CDMO環境中，冷藏室通常同時存放來自多個客戶的產品，裝載風險更為複雜：

  • 場景1：多客戶同時存取 — 不同班次的操作員頻繁進出，若無vinyl curtain，每次開門都會造成熱侵入
  • 場景2：大批量裝載進入 — 大量托盤同時裝入可能暫時阻擋冷風循環，形成局部熱點
  • 場景3：叉車進入造成氣流擾動 — 叉車引擎散熱 + 門口開啟同時發生，放大溫度衝擊
  • 場景4：非工作時間的最低頻率開門 — 凌晨班次進出頻率不同，代表最差情況(worst case)未必在白天

練習思考 1/3

Q：您的設施在進行冷藏室熱映射時，是否模擬了叉車進入及多次連續開門的場景？如果沒有，映射結果可能存在什麼風險？

提示：思考「驗證的場景」與「實際操作的場景」之間的差距（validation gap）對產品安全性的影響。

10

Chapter 10: Operational Issues | 操作問題

Section 10.2 — Open Door Recovery Test | 開門恢復測試

ISPE Source Text

10.2 Open Door Recovery Test

An example of a typical operational activity is to examine recovery time for the internal chamber temperature after opening the access door and simulating loading/unloading. It is recommended to determine the time that the chamber door may remain fully open before the monitoring sensors are no longer within the acceptable range.

This test can also help to determine how quickly the monitoring sensor recovers and returns to the normal operating temperature range.

Recommended Test Conditions

  • Use a minimum (simulated) load or no load — worst case with no thermal mass
  • Locate temperature sensors as recommended for thermal mapping, with special attention to sensors nearest the door
  • Set data acquisition rate to 1-minute intervals due to uncertainty in test duration

Acceptance Criteria

Generally, there are no specific acceptance criteria for this test unless a recovery time is specified in the unit manufacturer's specifications. The key output is a data-supported understanding of the chamber's tolerance for door-open events.

Special Case: Walk-in with Vinyl Curtains

For larger walk-in CTCs fitted with vinyl curtains, the units may be able to maintain internal conditions indefinitely, as the impact of passing through curtains is short-term and negligible. Vinyl curtains should be well-fitted, rest on the unit walls, and sit just clear of the floor.

中文解析 & CDMO應用

開門恢復測試詳解

為何選擇「最小/無負載」作為最差情況？

熱質量(thermal mass)越大，設備抵抗溫度波動的能力越強。若測試時使用空倉（最小熱質量），任何熱侵入都會被快速放大，反映最差情況。

這與工廠驗收測試(FAT/SAT)的邏輯一致：在最容易失敗的條件下驗證，通過才代表真正的品質保證。

開門緩衝時間 (Buffering Time) — 操作意義

開門恢復測試的關鍵輸出是開門允許時間上限，這個數字必須轉化為：

  • SOP中明確規定的「最大開門時間」
  • 作業員訓練的考核項目
  • CAPA追蹤的偏差觸發條件

如果SOP只寫「盡速關門」而沒有具體時間限制，等同於沒有控制。

開門事件對溫度影響示意
門打開 (T=0)
↓
熱侵入開始
最靠近門的感測器升溫
↓

練習思考 2/3

Q：您的SOP中是否明訂冷藏室最大開門時間？這個時間是基於開門恢復測試數據還是僅憑經驗設定？

延伸：若冷藏室安裝了vinyl curtain，開門時間限制是否可以放寬？放寬的前提是什麼？

Chapter 10: Operational Issues | 操作問題

Section 10.3 — Power Outage / Thermal Degradation Test | 停電/熱降解測試

ISPE Source Text

10.3 Power Outage / Thermal Degradation Test

Another type of test that may be helpful from a business continuity, disaster recovery, and operational perspective is a simulated Power Outage Test. This type of test would measure the amount of time the Controlled Temperature Chamber remained within the desired temperature range once electrical power was turned off.

Note: although it is expected the Controlled Temperature Chamber will have redundant and backup power supplies, the results from this test would provide data to define how quickly materials need to be moved to another location if the backup power systems failed. Doors to the storage chamber should remain closed during this test.

Recommended Test Setup

  • Use a minimum (simulated) load or no load in the CTC (worst case)
  • Perform as commissioning activity referenced in OQ before the storage unit is put into use, if possible
  • Locate temperature sensors as recommended for thermal mapping
  • Data acquisition rate: 1-minute intervals

Additional Operational Value

Once power is restored, the amount of time required to return to the appropriate required temperature can be of value for disaster recovery planning — specifically, the elapsed time from when power is restored until the last temperature sensor returns to the acceptable range.

Note: This test was previously included in the USP, but has subsequently been removed.

CDMO視角：停電測試的業務連續性價值

停電測試的輸出直接回答一個關鍵問題：
「如果備援電源完全失效，我有多少時間可以轉移產品？」

  • 2°C–8°C冷藏室：典型空倉衰減時間可能只有30–60分鐘
  • -20°C冷凍庫：空倉衰減時間可能達2–4小時（但滿倉更長）
  • 這些數據必須納入業務連續性計畫(BCP)和緊急應變程序(ERP)

練習思考 3/3

Q：您的設施是否有停電測試數據支撐緊急程序？如果備援電源在凌晨2點失效，值班人員能在多少分鐘內收到通知並採取行動？

情境延伸：若停電發生時冷藏室中存放的是某客戶的臨床試驗用藥，停電後2小時才發現，QA應如何評估產品可用性？

10

Chapter 10: Operational Issues | 操作問題

Sections 10.4–10.5 — Calibration Strategies, Access Control & Dehumidification | 校準策略、進出管制與除濕

ISPE Source Text

Calibration and Calibration Strategies

There are benefits to be derived from a considered calibration strategy:

  • Refrigeration system instruments: Many can only be calibrated when the system is emptied for major maintenance — therefore, they are calibrated following manufacturer recommendations
  • Control sensor: Can be verified at a single point, as the control functions are usually based on whether the system is above or below the operating set point
  • Monitoring sensors: Should be calibrated across the operating range, as they provide the data to support quality determinations in support of product quality

Access Control

Areas where product is stored should have a system to prevent unauthorized access. This system can be part of a site keycard system, or use a lock and key with procedural controls which identify who holds, and is entitled to use, the key.

Dehumidification

Dehumidification should be considered for a cold room or freezer. The life of the equipment can be extended where there are fewer defrost cycles required (reduced expansion/contraction). Dehumidification can also reduce the risk of ice forming on a freezer floor, which presents a safety hazard.

For large distribution facilities it may be worth considering the layout, and providing access to a walk-in freezer through a cold room, in order to reduce moisture in the freezer.

Equipment Durability

When specifying a new facility, it is worthwhile defining the system design life — the expected operating lifespan without significant maintenance. High quality refrigeration systems can have an expected life of 12 to 15 years. Standby systems are usually installed for an installation holding material of a significant commercial value.

中文解析 & CDMO應用

校準策略與進出管制深度解析

三層校準策略框架

關鍵原則：監測感測器的校準標準高於控制感測器，因為監測數據是產品放行的依據。

校準召回追蹤系統 (Calibration Recall System)

一個有效的校準召回系統應包含：

  • 儀器清冊(Asset Register)：每個感測器均有唯一ID、位置、校準週期、上次校準日期
  • 到期提醒：提前30天發送警示給校準工程師和QA
  • 逾期鎖定：超過校準有效期的感測器自動標記，其數據不得用於放行決策
  • 回溯評估：感測器超過校準期間若有偏差，需評估期間所有產品的影響
  • 替換驗證：校準後感測器重新安裝需確認讀值與同位置其他感測器的一致性

進出管制的GMP意義

進出管制不只是安全問題，也是GMP合規問題。未授權進入可能導致：

  • 產品被未記錄的方式取出（影響庫存完整性）
  • 不當操作造成溫度偏差（門被長時間打開）
  • 訪客接觸未貼標籤產品（交叉污染風險）

FDA 21 CFR Part 211.68 和 EU GMP Annex 15均要求儲存區域有適當的進出控制。

練習思考

Q：您的設施中，監測感測器(monitoring sensor)和控制感測器(control sensor)是否有不同的校準頻率規定？如果兩者都使用年度校準，這樣的做法是否符合ISPE的差異化要求？

11

Chapter 11: Packaged Transport Systems | 包裝運輸系統

Sections 11.1 — Active Shipping Containers: Unit Load Devices (ULD) | 主動式運輸容器：單位裝載設備

ISPE Source Text

11.1 Active Shipping Containers: Unit Load Devices

Currently there are two types of Unit Load Devices (ULD) systems suitable for the shipping of temperature sensitive product, designed for use in aircraft. They are powered to either cool or heat the air within the container.

System 1 (TCCU) Key Features

  • Maintains 5°C (41°F) for 72 hours at 30°C (86°F) ambient
  • Handles brief ambient excursions from -40°C to +60°C
  • GPS/GSM module for real-time location and temperature transmission
  • Two modes: recharge mode (connected to AC) and transport mode (24VDC battery)
  • Interior designed for 40×48 inch pallet, up to 500 kg product

System 2 Key Features

  • Maintains 5°C for 30 hours at -10°C to +30°C ambient
  • NiMH batteries; three cooling compressors with heaters
  • Supports US and EURO pallet sizes, up to 953 kg
  • LED alarm indicators: system on (green), charge (blue), alarm (red), alert (yellow)
  • Alert triggers: battery <30%, inside temp out of spec, ambient temp out of spec, compressor failure

11.1.3 Qualification Approaches

Two possible approaches for active shipping containers:

  • Unit Qualification: Map each individual unit; confirm satisfactory operation; qualify service supplier for maintenance and calibration quality systems
  • Supplier Assessment: (1) Qualify the manufacturer (design + factory testing); (2) Qualify service supplier (maintenance + calibration quality systems). Usually paired with an independent temperature logger per shipment.

Regardless of approach, loading and unloading methods must be qualified and procedurally defined. When unloading, shipment should be placed into quarantine until data logger confirms conditions were maintained. If out-of-conditions, a Non-Conformance must be raised and the implications investigated.

中文解析 & CDMO應用

主動式ULD運輸容器資格認證

單機資格 vs. 供應商評估：選擇邏輯

  • 選單機資格：當ULD由同一家供應商長期租用，數量固定，可針對每台設備建立獨立的資格文件。適合高價值/高風險產品。
  • 選供應商評估：當ULD數量龐大或頻繁更換，個別映射不切實際。透過審核製造商設計和服務商維護品質，輔以隨貨數據記錄器作為補充保證。
  • 關鍵補充措施：無論採哪種方法，每次運輸都應附帶獨立的溫度記錄器，這是最後一道確認機制。

冷鏈交接點 (Hand-off Points) 風險

從設施到最終目的地的冷鏈中，最脆弱的環節通常是交接點：

  • 設施倉庫 → 快遞取貨：產品在裝卸區暴露時間
  • 機場地面操作：從貨倉到飛機貨艙的轉移時間
  • 轉機點：兩段航班之間的等待時間
  • 目的地機場 → 客戶設施：最後一哩配送

每個交接點都應有明確的溫度確認程序和責任分工協議(Quality Agreement)。

練習思考

Q：您的設施在使用ULD運輸臨床試驗用藥時，採用的是單機資格還是供應商評估方式？隨貨溫度記錄器的數據是否有人系統性地審查，還是只在收貨時檢查一下就歸檔？

11

Chapter 11: Packaged Transport Systems | 包裝運輸系統

Sections 11.2–11.5 — Temperature Controlled Trailers: Design, Insulation & Validation | 溫控拖車：設計、隔熱與驗證

ISPE Source Text

11.2 Temperature Controlled Trailers

Temperature controlled over-the-road trailers can be used to move significant amounts of temperature sensitive pharmaceutical product. Trailers have a different set of environmental and usage profiles when compared to in situ custom-built CTCs:

  • Loading and unloading operations
  • Defrost cycles
  • Loading patterns

Moisture, as a degradation element, is much more prevalent in trailers due to the operational profile — continuous running for several days, followed by periods of downtime when the trailer is empty. Rigorous inspection of each trailer should be performed prior to loading.

11.3 Trailer Design

Product loaded into the trailer should be equilibrated to the appropriate temperature before loading. During transit, as heat or cold penetrates the walls, roof, and floor, circulating airflows capture the environmental heat or cold and condition it to the desired temperature in the HVAC unit on the front of the trailer.

Depending on the geographical area, manufacturers build and test trailers to meet standards of one of two organizations:

  • North America: American Trucking Association (ATA) Technology & Maintenance Council (TMC)
  • Europe: ATP Agreement on International Carriage of Perishable Foodstuffs

TMC / ATP Classification Table

11.4 Insulation Degradation

Polyurethane foam insulation gradually loses its blowing agent gas (CO₂ and other gases) over time, which is replaced with air and water vapor. This transition occurs slowly over years and is normal. The temperature control unit is sized to assure a useful life of 15 years with timely maintenance.

11.5 Trailer Validation Approach

The validation exercise is focused on loading patterns and assuring that proper airflow can be achieved under conditions of heat and cold. Loading practices that block airflow impede heat addition/removal and result in product temperatures that may not be controlled within the required range. A written protocol should document temperatures nearest the product during seasonal extremes.

中文解析 & CDMO應用

溫控拖車驗證策略與CTC比較

比喻：為什麼F級拖車成功也意味著DF級會成功？

ISPE指出，在F級拖車上成功完成的驗證研究，也意味著DF級(深冷凍)拖車同樣適用。

這就像汽車安全測試：如果一輛配備標準安全設備的車通過了碰撞測試，那麼裝備更多安全功能的高配版車款自然也能通過 — 因為F級是市場主流且絕緣能力更低，通過代表更高標準的DF也能達標。

隔熱衰退的實務意義

聚氨酯泡沫的隔熱性能會隨時間下降（發泡劑氣體逸散 → 空氣和水蒸氣取代），這意味著：

  • 新拖車的初始性能 ≠ 使用5–10年後的性能
  • 驗證研究應考慮設備年齡和使用歷史
  • 定期熱掃描(thermal scanning)可早期發現隔熱劣化
  • 質量協議應要求承運商定期提供拖車維護記錄

練習思考

Q：您的設施使用溫控拖車進行產品配送時，是否與承運商簽訂品質協議？該協議是否涵蓋拖車的TMC/ATP認證等級要求、定期檢查標準，以及溫度超規時的通報程序？

11

Chapter 11: Packaged Transport Systems | 包裝運輸系統

Section 11.6 — Trailer Loading Patterns & Inspectional Criteria | 拖車裝載模式與檢查標準

ISPE Source Text

11.6 Trailer Loading Patterns

Loading patterns in a well maintained truck are the key determinant in assuring even product temperature within the trailer. Key requirements:

  • Product should be loaded on pallets that allow free airflow the length of the trailer
  • Product should not be in contact with the walls of the trailer
  • Double stacking of refrigerated goods should be carefully considered, as airflow distribution in the rear of the trailer may not be sufficient to maintain uniform temperature under extreme conditions
  • Product should be equilibrated to the appropriate temperature before loading

11.6.1 Inspectional Criteria

The Quality Agreement between the carrier and the company should define the shared responsibilities of inspection. The following items should be inspected for each use:

  • Air distribution chute intact
  • Air supply, air returns and floor drains clear of debris
  • Repairs to interior and exterior surfaces (damage from forklifts etc.)
  • Door seals intact
  • General cleanliness (visual inspection)
中文解析 & CDMO應用

裝載模式對溫度均一性的關鍵影響

裝載模式的三大原則

  • 原則1 — 氣流暢通：托盤之間必須保留足夠間距讓冷空氣循環，阻擋氣流等同於阻擋溫度調節能力
  • 原則2 — 不接觸側壁：拖車側壁是熱交換最強的區域（尤其夏季），接觸側壁的產品最容易超出溫度範圍
  • 原則3 — 預冷後才裝載：裝載未冷卻至目標溫度的產品，等同於在拖車內引入一個熱源，增加冷機負擔

每次使用前的拖車檢查清單

  • 空氣分配導管(air distribution chute)完整無損
  • 送風口、回風口、地板排水孔無堵塞
  • 內外側壁無叉車造成的穿孔或凹陷
  • 門封條(door seals)完整，無裂縫或破損
  • 整體清潔度符合要求（無異物、無前次貨物殘留）
  • 冷機組(reefer unit)正常運轉，設定點正確
  • 拖車內部溫度已達到目標範圍
  • TMC/ATP認證標牌可見且在有效期內

練習思考

Q：您的設施在出貨前是否有書面的拖車檢查記錄？若承運商提供的拖車門封條出現輕微裂縫但拖車溫度仍在範圍內，您會如何決策：使用這台拖車還是要求更換？

提示：思考「當下合格」與「長途運輸過程中的潛在風險」之間的平衡。

Chapter 12: Maintenance | 維護

Sections 12.1–12.4 — Coils, Condensate, Functional Testing & Leak Testing | 盤管、冷凝管、功能測試與洩漏測試

ISPE Source Text

Chapter 12 Maintenance — Overview

The supplier of the refrigeration equipment should provide general recommendations for the maintenance of the equipment. These recommendations may not recognize the high value of the stored goods in this application. The potential impact on the maintenance program should be assessed.

12.1 Cleaning of the Coils

The coils (unit cooler and air cooled condenser) should be cleaned regularly and checked for any damage to ensure that performance levels are maintained. Damaged or distorted fins should be straightened with a suitable comb. This inspection should also ensure that there is no corrosion of the fins.

Regular inspection should also confirm that the defrost cycle is effective (where applicable), especially if the cycle is adjusted to account for seasonal variation.

General Cleaning: Dry cleaning is preferred, in order to minimize risk of contamination. Regular inspection is recommended to ensure that there is no unseen microbial/fungicidal growth.

12.2 Check the Condensate Pipework

The condensate pipework should be checked to ensure that it is not damaged and that it has the correct fall and flows freely. Trace heating or insulation also should be checked. Periodic verification during operation is also recommended; this should ensure that the pipe supports are adequate and have not loosened.

12.3 Functional Testing of Unit Coolers / Defrost Elements

There is usually no feedback from the solenoid valve on the unit coolers, so the only way of checking their correct operation is to carry out, periodically, a functional check to verify the performance of each unit cooler.

12.4 Leak Testing

  • Periodically check pipe runs and equipment for leaks using electronic test devices
  • Check refrigerant fluid level and pressure against system specification — early detection may help avoid system failure
  • Keep a record of refrigerant used for the system (may be mandatory depending on region)
  • Equipment rooms may be fitted with leakage detectors/alarms — these should be calibrated and checked regularly
  • End Users should be aware of local regulatory requirements
中文解析 & CDMO應用

盤管、冷凝管與洩漏測試詳解

關鍵洞察：製造商建議 ≠ GMP要求

ISPE明確指出，設備製造商的維護建議通常不考慮高價值藥品儲存的特殊需求。這意味著：

  • 製造商建議可能是基於食品或一般工業應用
  • GMP環境下的維護頻率和標準必須由使用方（CDMO）自行評估和設定
  • 維護計畫必須考慮「若此設備失效，對產品品質的影響是什麼？」

這正是風險基礎的PM計畫的基礎：設備關鍵性 → 決定維護頻率和深度。

盤管清潔的微生物風險

ISPE推薦乾式清潔(dry cleaning)而非濕式清潔，原因是：

  • 濕式清潔引入水分，可能在盤管翼片(fins)上形成生物膜(biofilm)滋生環境
  • 冷藏室的低溫並非無菌環境 — 某些嗜冷菌(psychrotrophic bacteria)和黴菌在2–8°C下仍可緩慢生長
  • 微生物污染的盤管可能通過氣流將孢子傳播至儲存產品的環境

冷媒洩漏記錄的法規要求

許多地區對冷媒使用和洩漏有強制性記錄要求：

  • 歐盟 F-Gas Regulation (EU 517/2014)：含氟冷媒超過一定量需定期洩漏檢查並記錄
  • EPA Section 608 (美國)：ODS冷媒洩漏超過閾值需修復並記錄
  • GMP視角：冷媒洩漏可能污染產品，且洩漏事件可能影響設備效能，進而影響儲存溫度

冷媒記錄(refrigerant log)應成為PM文件系統的一部分。

練習思考

Q：您的冷藏設備上次盤管清潔是什麼時候？清潔記錄是否包含了「清潔前/後目視檢查結果」以及清潔方法？如果不是乾式清潔，是否評估過微生物污染風險？

12

Chapter 12: Maintenance | 維護

Sections 12.5–12.6 — Thermal Scanning & System Alarms | 熱掃描與系統警報

ISPE Source Text

12.5 Thermal Scanning

The panels, doors, door seals, and sealing of utility penetrations can degrade over time (foamed panels may be better in this respect than panels filled with mineral wool). A thermal scan of the installation will allow any degradation to be seen and appropriate action taken.

As a minimum, the penetrations should be visually inspected to ensure that they are sound with no leakage/ingress of condensation. For conduit penetrations, the internal sealing also should be checked to ensure that condensation is not leaking inside the conduit.

12.6 System Alarms

The entire alarm system should be periodically tested by direct or simulated temperature change against the specified alarm set points and proper functionality of audible and visual alarms at local and/or remote alarm stations (e.g., emails, phone calls, or text based alerts) should be confirmed and documented.

Regardless of the root cause, product losses from cold storage-related failures can be prevented with the proper design and operation of the alarm system, and proper End User response to an alarm event. Periodic testing of the alarm system should help to ensure that it will work when needed.

The system maintenance procedures can be used to provide a confirmation that the system performance remains satisfactory, supporting a reduced requirement for remapping where appropriate. The data from the monitoring system should be reviewed periodically, to look for any negative performance trends.

中文解析 & CDMO應用

熱掃描、警報系統與重新映射觸發條件

熱掃描(Thermal Scanning) — 非破壞性隔熱檢測

紅外熱成像(Infrared Thermography)可在不拆除板材的情況下，透過溫度差異識別隔熱劣化區域：

  • 正常隔熱：表面溫度均勻，無明顯熱橋
  • 隔熱劣化：面板某區域出現「熱點」，代表冷橋或隔熱材料受損
  • 門封條洩漏：門框周圍出現溫度梯度異常
  • 管道穿牆處：若密封不良，凝結水會沿管道滲入

建議：熱掃描應在設備滿載運行時進行，內外溫差最大，最容易發現問題。

警報測試的GMP要求

「定期測試警報」不只是技術要求，更是GMP合規要求。一個從未被測試的警報系統，在真正需要時可能完全失效。

  • 測試方式：直接溫度變化（模擬真實偏差）或受控模擬（注入測試信號）
  • 測試範圍：本地聲光警報 + 遠端通報（Email/SMS/Phone）
  • 文件要求：測試結果必須記錄，包含測試時間、觸發條件、通報到達時間
  • Response time目標：從警報觸發到有人確認，應有明確的期望時間

維護數據 → 減少重新映射需求

ISPE提供了一個重要的生命週期管理原則：如果系統維護記錄良好，且監測數據顯示性能穩定，可以減少重新熱映射的頻率。

這需要SME（主題專家）定期審查：

  • 監測數據趨勢 vs. 資格認證時的基準數據
  • 警報歷史記錄（是否出現新的偏差模式？）
  • 維護歷史（是否有影響性能的重大維修？）
  • 設備年齡和隔熱衰退評估

相反地，若出現以下情況，必須觸發重新映射：重大維修更換（壓縮機、冷凝器）、設備搬遷、性能數據顯示明顯趨勢偏移。

練習思考

Q：您的設施上次警報系統測試是什麼時候？測試記錄是否涵蓋了遠端通報渠道（SMS/Email）的響應確認？若值班人員更換了手機號碼，警報通報系統是否會自動更新？

12

Chapter 12: Maintenance | 維護

PM by Equipment Type + Calibration Recall System + PM Frequency Table | 依設備類型的PM程序 + 校準召回系統 + PM頻率表

ISPE Source Text

PM Procedures by Equipment Type

CRT Storage Area (Warehouse)

  1. Inspect building envelope — no visible degradation of materials of construction or seals/curtains that would impact ingress of unconditioned air
  2. Review system alarm history since last maintenance (temperature monitoring system, HVAC temperature/humidity, airflow volume sensors) — look for negative performance trends
  3. Visually check HVAC system balance — verify balancing dampers remain in their as-commissioned/marked settings
  4. Check and clean heating/cooling coils if necessary
  5. Check control system records — confirm control valves are not operating at 100% (indicating performance limits or utility system issues)

Walk-in Refrigerators / Freezers

  1. Inspect system envelope — no visible degradation, door/window seals, door curtains, or air leakage paths (moisture or ice buildup)
  2. Review system alarm history (temperature monitoring + refrigeration system alarms) — note observations in maintenance record
  3. Check refrigeration system set point being maintained (e.g., compressor suction pressure)
  4. Review maintenance history to confirm:
    • Coils have been cleaned if needed
    • Fan operation has been checked
    • Operation of unit cooler control valves and thermal expansion valves checked
    • Defrost settings and operation verified (if applicable)

Standalone Refrigerators and Freezers

Same four-point checklist as walk-in units (envelope inspection, alarm history review, set point verification, maintenance history review for coils / fans / valves / defrost).

Performance Review by SME (Alternative to Full PM)

Where a system has multiple monitoring locations (control sensor + independent temperature monitor at hot/cold spots), the preventive maintenance is not required to confirm satisfactory unit operation in every cycle. Instead:

A review of current system performance data against the as-Qualified data by an SME can be used to confirm consistent system performance. This review should assess the thermal performance of unit insulation and the conditioning system, allowing the SME to determine if there has been a significant change in performance that may require maintenance activities, or if the system is still performing acceptably.

中文解析 & PM計畫設計

預防性維護計畫要素與頻率表

PM頻率建議表 | PM Frequency Reference

PM計畫完整要素清單

  • 設備清冊：每台設備有唯一ID、型號、安裝日期、關鍵性等級
  • PM時間表：基於設備關鍵性和製造商建議的頻率設定
  • PM工作單(Work Order)：清晰的步驟指示、所需工具和備件
  • 維護記錄：每次PM的執行人、日期、發現事項、措施
  • 逾期PM追蹤：PM逾期時的升級通報機制
  • PM影響評估：重大PM對溫度映射有效性的影響評估
  • 備件管理：關鍵備件庫存（過濾器、密封條、保險絲）
  • 供應商認證：外包維護供應商的資格和品質協議
  • 校準整合：PM時同步確認感測器校準狀態
  • CAPA整合：PM中發現的問題直接進入CAPA系統

溫度偏差評估決策樹

Temperature Excursion Assessment Protocol | 溫度超規評估流程

溫度偏差(Excursion)產品影響評估決策樹
1. 警報觸發或監測數據顯示溫度超規 — 是否已記錄偏差時間和持續時間？
否 → 立即記錄發現時間，估算最長可能暴露時間（最差情況）
是 → 進入步驟2
2. 超規溫度和持續時間是否在產品說明書(SmPC)的允許累積暴露範圍內？
是 → 記錄評估結論，確認後續監測加強，開立輕微偏差報告
否 → 進入步驟3（產品隔離）
3. 立即隔離涉及批次，通知QA和產品SME，開立主要偏差報告
4. 是否有已核准的超標穩定性數據(out-of-storage stability data)支撐產品可用性？
是 → QA審查數據，若支持 → 有條件放行或縮短有效期
否 → 進入步驟5
5. 是否可進行額外穩定性測試評估產品品質？
是 → 送樣測試，結果支持則有條件放行，否則廢棄
否 → 廢棄受影響批次，完整CAPA分析，根本原因調查
6. 無論最終決定，必須識別根本原因並實施CAPA，評估是否需要觸發重新映射

練習思考（綜合題）

情境：週五深夜，2°C–8°C冷藏室溫度升至12°C，持續了4小時才有人察覺。室內存放了3個批次的生物製劑原液，其中一批是客戶即將用於III期臨床試驗的關鍵批次。

Q1：您的第一個行動是什麼？（提示：思考時間線重建）

Q2：產品說明書上寫「2–8°C儲存，避免超過25°C」，這是否足以判定這4小時偏差是否影響產品品質？

Q3：這次偏差是否應觸發冷藏室重新映射？判斷依據是什麼？

PM事件對映射有效性的影響評估 | PM Impact on Qualification Status

✓

Section Summary & Key Takeaways | 章節總結與關鍵要點

Chapters 10–12 Integrated Learning | 第10–12章整合學習

Key Messages from Chapters 10–12

Chapter 10 Core Takeaways

  • Operational realism: Mapping studies must include real operational activities — door openings, equipment operation, loading simulation — to be valid
  • Open door recovery: Test under empty (worst-case) conditions; 1-minute data acquisition; outputs inform SOP time limits
  • Power outage: Empty-chamber degradation data = the clock that governs your emergency response window
  • Calibration differentiation: Monitoring sensors need full-range multi-point calibration; control sensors only need single-point verification
  • Access control: Unauthorized access is a GMP deficiency, not just a security issue

Chapter 11 Core Takeaways

  • ULD qualification: Two approaches — individual unit mapping or supplier assessment system. Either way, an independent in-shipment logger is essential
  • Trailer as a CTC: Trailers are a mobile subclass of CTCs, with additional challenges from moisture, loading patterns, and road vibration
  • TMC/ATP standards: Industry standards provide a "family" qualification basis — an F-rated trailer study covers DF as well
  • Airflow is everything: Loading patterns that block airflow are the leading cause of temperature non-uniformity in trailers
  • Pre-shipment inspection: Every trailer, every time — document it per the Quality Agreement

Chapter 12 Core Takeaways

  • Manufacturer ≠ GMP: Equipment supplier maintenance recommendations do not account for high-value pharmaceutical storage — you must set your own risk-based standards
  • Dry clean coils: Moisture introduced during wet cleaning creates microbial growth risk in cold environments
  • Alarm testing is non-negotiable: Periodic testing of the full alarm pathway (local + remote) is a GMP requirement, not optional
  • Good maintenance can reduce re-mapping: Consistent PM + SME trend review can justify extended intervals between full thermal mapping studies
  • Major repairs trigger re-qualification: Compressor replacement, unit cooler change, controller replacement — all require re-assessment

整合應用：CDMO Operations Director視角

"A mapped chamber that isn't maintained properly is a mapped chamber that no longer reflects reality."
「已完成映射但維護不當的設備，其映射結果已無法反映現實。」

從運營總監角度的三個核心問責問題

  1. 操作合規性：我的團隊在每次開門、裝載、進出冷藏室時，是否都遵循了基於映射數據制定的SOP？是否有監控機制確保合規？
  2. 維護完整性：我的PM計畫是否真正基於設備關鍵性設計？最近一次PM逾期是什麼時候？逾期期間的產品狀態是否有評估？
  3. 系統可靠性：如果今晚凌晨3點發生停電，我的警報系統是否會在5分鐘內通知到正確的人？我有多久沒有測試這個假設了？

映射 → 操作 → 維護的生命週期閉環

熱映射建立基準
(Thermal Mapping)
↓

SOP開門時間、裝載規範
↓
PM計畫維持設備性能
確保映射條件不改變
↓
定期SME性能審查

最終綜合思考題

場景：您剛接任CDMO的QA副總裁職位，被要求在90天內評估冷鏈GMP合規狀態。

基於Chapters 10–12，您的前15天優先審查清單包含哪些？

請思考：(1) 操作合規性文件審查 (2) PM記錄完整性 (3) 校準召回狀態 (4) 警報測試記錄 (5) 最近偏差的根本原因分析品質 (6) 承運商品質協議覆蓋範圍

Chapter 5: Appendix 1: Example URS

附錄1：用戶需求規格書範例 | p87-p100

ISPE Good Practice Guide — CTC Mapping & Monitoring (2016)

Appendix 1 (Part 1): Example URS — Facility & Performance Requirements

附錄1（第一部分）：設施與性能需求 — 用戶需求規格範例
Source: Appendix 1 / Section 13 · pp. 62–68

Contents — 本節目錄

1. URS Structure & Purpose 2. Regulatory Requirements 3. Capacity & Construction 4. Process Requirements 5. Sample URS: Scope & Definitions 6. Sample URS: System Description 7. Sample URS: Capacity Requirements 8. Good vs. Poor URS Comparison

Learning Objectives — 學習目標

English

  • Identify the mandatory components of a GMP-compliant URS
  • Distinguish regulatory vs. operational vs. business requirements
  • Apply testability criteria to screen URS statements
  • Describe how facility context shapes cold-room requirements
  • Structure a URS section map for a walk-in cold room

中文

  • 識別符合GMP的URS必要組成項目
  • 區分法規、操作與業務三類需求的差異
  • 用「可測試性」標準篩選URS條文
  • 說明設施背景如何影響冷藏室需求
  • 為步入式冷藏室建立URS章節架構
"A URS requirement must be testable — if you can't write a test for it, you haven't written a requirement."
URS需求必須可被驗證——若無法為它設計測試，那你寫的只是一段說明，不是需求。
1

URS Structure & Purpose — URS的結構與目的

What a URS must contain and why it drives the entire qualification lifecycle

13.1.1 Purpose (Source Text)

Purpose: The purpose of this document is to provide the system developer with the user's requirements for the x°C freezer.

Overview

Text goes here [facility-specific context to be completed by the user].

Background

Text goes here [product types, storage history, regulatory context].

Key Objectives

The system will store GMP material at x°C to x°C.

Main Functions

The system shall be capable of storing material at x°C to x°C and provide a general system fault alarm and high and low alarm set points that can interface with the monitoring system. The monitoring system will provide the quality system alarms and provide operator paging.

A complete URS typically includes:

  • Purpose and scope
  • Definitions and abbreviations
  • References (regulations, standards)
  • System description
  • User requirements (capacity, process, automation)
  • Design and construction constraints
  • Operations and maintenance

解說與CDMO應用 Commentary

為什麼URS如此關鍵？

URS是整個設備資格驗證的起點。IQ/OQ/PQ的每一個測試項目都應回溯至URS中的特定需求。若URS寫得模糊，後續驗證就無從追溯。

URS的三層需求

  • 法規需求 (Regulatory): 21 CFR Part 11、EU GMP Annex 11 — 必須滿足，不可妥協
  • 業務需求 (Business): 容積、電力規格 — 來自操作現實
  • 操作需求 (Operational): 排班方式、清潔週期 — 決定日常使用限制

CDMO多客戶情境

CDMO環境中，同一台冷藏室可能存放多個客戶的GMP材料，每位客戶對溫度範圍、進出頻率、鑑別系統的要求不同。URS必須反映「最嚴格的共同標準」，而非單一客戶需求。

常見陷阱

"The system shall maintain proper temperature" — 這不是需求，是期望。正確寫法：「系統須將內部溫度維持在2°C至8°C，在最大負載條件下穩定時間不超過30分鐘。」

Practice Questions 練習思考

  1. 一份URS的「目的」欄位說「提供GMP儲存空間」——請指出至少兩個問題，並改寫。
  2. CDMO同時服務兩個客戶，客戶A要求2–8°C、客戶B要求-20°C。如何在同一份URS中處理這個衝突？
  3. 「主要功能」提到monitoring system提供paging。這項需求屬於哪一層（法規/業務/操作）？為什麼？
2

Applicable GMP Requirements & Regulations — 適用GMP法規要求

How regulatory citations translate into testable URS statements

13.1.1 Regulatory Section (Source Text)

Applicable GMP Requirements and Regulations:

  • 21 CFR Part 11 Compliance (if the system provides an electronic record)
  • Relevant regulations — see Section 1.4 of the Guide
Guide Note: The specific application may have requirements defined related to the regulations, rather than defining the regulation itself — e.g., "each storage location must have a bar code label defining the location for the inventory management system."

解說與CDMO應用 Commentary

不要只列法規名稱

直接引用「21 CFR Part 11」不算需求——你必須說明哪個具體要求適用於這套系統。例如：「電子溫度記錄不可被修改，修改必須留下審計軌跡（audit trail）」。

CDMO常見適用法規

  • 21 CFR Part 11 — 電子記錄/電子簽章（若系統產生ER/ES）
  • EU GMP Annex 11 — 電腦化系統驗證
  • ICH Q9 — 風險管理（影響警報優先級設定）
  • USP <1079> — 良好儲存與運輸實踐

Guide的聰明建議

將法規轉化為業務語言。「有條碼標示的儲存位置」比「符合庫存管理系統要求」更具體、更可測試。這是ISPE指南的核心立場：requirements should be outcome-focused, not regulation-quoting.

3

Capacity, Pallet Racking & Construction — 容積、棧板架與建造需求

Operational requirements that define physical specifications

13.1.2 Operational Requirements (Source Text)

Capacity

  • 12 Euro pallets (X by Y by Z)
  • System maximum single shipment loaded into the unit is 4 pallets (Note: product is at storage temperature)
  • System load removed in single pallet units

Pallet Racking

  • Racking is to be GMP grade cleanable crevice free with a finish that is resistant to cleaning, sanitizing, and sporicidal agents

Safety

The unit must be fitted with:

  • Internal emergency lighting
  • A mechanism to allow door opening from the inside of the unit regardless of the lock status
  • An internal alarm button connected to a suitable alarm system

解說與CDMO應用 Commentary

容積需求的計算邏輯

「12個Euro棧板」必須綁定到實際尺寸（X×Y×Z）。若URS只寫數量而沒有尺寸，供應商可能設計出形狀無法放入任何標準棧板的空間。

單次入庫量的重要性

「最大單次入庫4棧板」是一個關鍵的熱負荷（thermal load）參數。這個數字直接影響OQ中的溫度恢復時間測試設計。若URS未定義，驗證就無法設計最差情況（worst case）。

GMP Grade棧板架的實際要求

「無縫隙（crevice free）」和「耐殺孢劑（sporicidal agents）」是具體可測試的材料規格。可接受PVC塗層鋼架或不鏽鋼，但需在DQ階段提供材料證明。

安全需求不只是OSHA問題

「從內側開門」的機制是法規要求，但在CDMO場所更需要考慮：操作員進入冷藏室時是否有人員追蹤系統？緊急按鈕連接的警報是否覆蓋24小時？

Practice Questions 練習思考

  1. 「最大單次入庫4棧板」這項需求，應該在OQ的哪個測試中被驗證？請設計測試標題與接受標準。
  2. 若CDMO有兩個客戶，一個用Euro棧板、一個用美式棧板，URS應如何處理這個差異？
  3. 「耐殺孢劑」需求如何在DQ文件中被確認？需要哪些供應商文件？
4

Process, Monitoring & Automation Requirements — 製程、監控與自動化需求

Temperature control, alarms, data integrity, and system interfaces

13.1.2 Process & System Requirements (Source Text)

Process Requirements

  • Include allowable excursions (e.g., specific product may be exposed to high temps up to x°C for y minutes if MKT does not exceed z°C)
  • Maintain operating rate of x°C to x°C — expected results
  • Maintain operating range of x°C to x°C — acceptance criteria
  • Factory installed access port for installation of temperature mapping sensors

Note: MKT is not generally used for cold rooms or freezers, but is commonly applied to controlled room temperature storage.

Independent Temperature Monitoring System

  • High and low temperature alarm and paging to alert staff in the event of an excursion

Automation System Functions

  • Local display of operational status, temperature, and alarm conditions
  • Access control security to the panel and set points
  • Local audible/visual alarms for high, low, high-high, and low-low temperatures and general system fault
  • Factory installed access port for installation of temperature mapping sensors
  • Critical alarms displayed at X; Non-critical alarms displayed at Y

Alarms Classification

Data and Security

  • Data storage capacity requirements
  • Security access requirements
  • Archive requirements
  • Data Security and Integrity — recorded data cannot be modified

解說與CDMO應用 Commentary

「作業範圍」vs「驗收標準」的區別

URS中必須明確區分：operating rate（設備目標操作溫度）vs operating range（接受標準/規格上下限）。這兩者分別對應OQ的正常操作驗證與PQ的最差情況驗證。

警報系統架構的GMP意義

  • Level 1（Low/High）: 提醒操作員注意趨勢
  • Level 2（Low-Low/High-High）: 需要立即行動的GMP偏差
  • DCS整合: 確保警報記錄進入21 CFR Part 11管轄的審計軌跡

獨立監控系統的重要性

URS特別要求「獨立」（independent）的溫度監控系統。這意味著監控傳感器不能與設備的控制感測器共用電路——兩個系統必須能夠互相驗證。這是FDA檢查員常見的查核點。

感測器接口（Access Port）

要求「出廠時預裝感測器接口」是一個聰明的設計選擇。若在冷藏室建造完成後才鑽孔安裝接口，需要重新驗證密封完整性，既費時又有風險。

資料完整性：「不可修改」要如何驗證？

「記錄數據不可被修改」必須在URS中補充：（1）系統如何防止修改（技術控制），（2）若需更正如何留下審計記錄（21 CFR Part 11 §11.10(e)）。這兩點都需要在OQ中測試。

Practice Questions 練習思考

  1. URS中要求「High-High alarm」，請寫出這個警報的具體觸發條件（溫度值）和系統回應（需要哪些自動動作？）
  2. 「獨立監控系統」與設備控制系統需要分開驗證嗎？各需要什麼文件？
  3. 若CDMO客戶要求數據存取日誌（access log），這應該放在URS哪個子章節？屬於哪一層需求？
5

Sample URS — Sections 1–3: Scope, Definitions & References — 範例URS：範圍、定義與參考文件

How to write the front matter of a URS that will survive regulatory scrutiny

Section 1 — General: Purpose and Scope (Source Text)

The purpose of this document is to define the user requirements for a walk-in Cold Room to be installed at the XYZ facility.

The user requirements stated herein describe what must be achieved for the system to serve its intended purpose. This document is not intended to be prescriptive as to how those user requirements are met. Revise this document to reflect changes that occur throughout the system life cycle and update it to document the current system requirements.

Section 2 — Definitions and Abbreviations

Key abbreviations: BMS, CE, dB(A), MCC, OSHA, PI, RTD, SCBD, SME, SOP, UPS, URS, VAC

Section 3 — References

[Document Identifier] — [Title] (to be completed with applicable regulatory documents and site SOPs)

解說與CDMO應用 Commentary

「描述要達成什麼，不是如何達成」

範例URS第1節清楚說明：這份文件不規定如何達成需求。這是URS與DS（Design Specification）的核心差異。若URS開始指定品牌、型號或工程方法，就越界了。

Living Document原則

URS應隨設備生命週期更新。CDMO常見問題：設備使用5年後功能擴充，但URS從未更新，導致後續驗證失去追溯依據。建議在URS末尾設立「Change Summary」章節（範例已包含此節）。

定義章節的作用

CDMO與客戶常因術語不一致產生誤解。在URS中明確定義「SME」的組成（QA、工程、驗證、生產）可以避免後續驗收時的責任爭議。RTD的定義對於監控傳感器類型選擇至關重要。

References節不能留空

許多公司在此填「N/A」。實際上應列出：適用的FDA指引、EU GMP附錄、場所SOP編號、以及設備供應商的技術標準。這些文件是DQ期間的核心審查資料。

6

Sample URS — Section 4: System Description — 系統描述

Defining system boundaries and physical components

Section 4 — System Description (Source Text)

The walk-in Cold Room units provide refrigerated storage for XX that support production.

This system encompasses the equipment items listed below, as illustrated by referenced P&IDs:

The Cold Room will comprise of:

  • Prefabricated insulated wall panels and roof
  • Insulated floor slab
  • Lights, emergency lights, automated door, emergency exit door (actuated by a manual push bar)
  • Evaporators
  • Refrigeration skids
  • Refrigeration piping between refrigeration skids and evaporators
  • Piping, instruments, controls, and safety features required for operation

The Cold Room unit will be controlled locally with the vendor supplied control system, interfacing with operations personnel via the vendor supplied OIT and hand switches. It is integrated with the site BMS to allow for performance monitoring, data archiving, and alarming.

解說與CDMO應用 Commentary

System Description的驗證功能

這個章節定義了系統邊界（System Classification Boundary）。邊界內的設備都需要被納入驗證範圍（IQ）。注意：冷藏系統與BMS的介面（interface）也需要被驗證，包括數據傳輸的正確性與完整性。

P&ID的重要性

「TBA（To Be Announced）」P&ID在URS階段是可接受的。但在DQ結束前必須確定P&ID編號，因為IQ需要以實際P&ID為基礎進行安裝確認。

CDMO的BMS整合挑戰

CDMO場所通常有多個客戶的設備共用BMS。URS應明確指出：冷藏室數據在BMS中的存取權限設定（哪些客戶可以看到哪些警報）以及數據隔離要求。

「緊急出口門由手動推桿啟動」

這個設計規格看似簡單，但需要在IQ中驗證安裝正確，在OQ中測試功能（包括停電情況下）。若URS沒有列出這個元件，可能被遺漏在驗證範圍之外。

7

Sample URS — Section 5: Capacity & Product Requirements — 容積與產品需求

Translating business needs into traceable, numbered requirements

5.1 Process Requirements: Capacity (Source Text)

5.2 Process Requirements: Product Physical Properties

[To be completed: product types, weight per pallet, temperature excursion limits for each product category stored in this unit.]

解說與CDMO應用 Commentary

編號需求（Numbered Requirements）的價值

URS 5.1、5.2、5.3等編號是驗證追蹤矩陣（Traceability Matrix）的基礎。每個IQ/OQ/PQ測試項目都必須指向至少一個URS ID。若需求沒有編號，可追溯性就無法建立。

"Should" vs "Shall" vs "Must"

  • Shall / Must: 強制需求，驗證必須確認
  • Should: 建議/目標，可接受例外但需記錄理由

5.2使用「should」（設計條件）而5.1使用「must」（硬性要求）——這個語言選擇是刻意的，CDMO工程師需要理解其差異。

外部設計條件（External Design Conditions）

-2.8°C至36.7°C的外部溫度範圍來自ASHRAE標準，代表設備所在地區（如美國）的氣候極值。這個數字影響冷藏系統的冷凍容量（refrigeration capacity）計算——是IQ的基礎技術參數。

「地板不儲存物料」的GMP意義

不放地板是GMP預防措施（防潮、防污染、便於清潔）。但URS必須進一步指定：「所有貨架底部離地至少X公分，提供清潔工具進入空間。」這樣才算可測試的需求。

Practice Questions 練習思考

  1. 需求5.2使用「should」，若供應商無法達到-2.8°C的外部設計條件，需要什麼文件來記錄這個例外？
  2. 5.2的「Product Physical Properties」章節在CDMO環境下應包含哪些欄位？請列出至少5項。
  3. 如何在追蹤矩陣中將URS 5.1連結到OQ測試？請寫出對應的OQ測試標題。
8

Good vs. Poor URS Requirement — 好需求與差需求對照表

Five real-world examples showing what testable requirements look like

The table below illustrates the principle: every URS statement must be verifiable. A poor requirement describes an intent; a good requirement defines a measurable outcome. 以下對照表體現核心原則：每條URS陳述必須可被驗證。差需求描述意圖；好需求定義可量化的結果。

"A URS requirement must be testable — if you can't write a test for it, you haven't written a requirement."
URS需求必須可被驗證——若無法為它設計測試，那你寫的只是一段說明，不是需求。

Appendix 1 (Part 2): Example URS — Monitoring, Qualification & Documentation Requirements

附錄1（第二部分）：監測、確效與文件要求 | URS Example Continued

Controlled Temperature Chamber Mapping and Monitoring (2016)  |  Source: Appendix 1, pp. 69–72

Learning Objectives / 學習目標

  1. Interpret the automation and alarm requirements in a URS for a controlled temperature chamber (CTC). / 解讀受控溫度腔體URS中的自動化與警報要求。
  2. Explain the IQ/OQ/PQ qualification phases and link each URS requirement to the appropriate phase. / 說明IQ/OQ/PQ確效階段，並將URS要求連結至對應階段。
  3. Construct a URS-to-qualification traceability matrix for a cold room system. / 建立冷藏室系統的URS至確效可追溯矩陣。
  4. Identify the documentation deliverables a supplier must provide post-installation. / 識別供應商安裝後必須提供的文件交付物。
